Current Commentary

Consistency in Grain Policy

— Liu

Recently, the Shanghai grain market has once again stirred up a major uproar. First, Jiading County detained more than two hundred grain boats passing through, almost rendering the Zhabei rice market non-existent. However, because of the provisional regulatory measures passed by the Executive Yuan this month, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, at its meeting on the 8th, decided to abolish the provincial regulations strictly prohibiting the export of food grains on a temporary basis and instructed Jiading County to release the grain boats. This issue has been generally resolved. The release of grain boats detained in Yueqing, Zhejiang Province, is also expected to be unproblematic.

Second, the price of flour and wheat has been rising endlessly, with prices even reaching a limit of one dime several times. According to yesterday's closing market prices, forward (April) flour has already gone up to four dollars and one dime, and wheat is also above seven dollars. Such a frenzied surge is, aside from other issues, bound to lead to a price increase for noodles, which cost 240 cash per catty. This has a significant impact on the livelihoods of ordinary people.

Third, the persistent rise in the price of coarse grains and oil beans is also a matter of great concern. Since the loss of the four northeastern provinces, China has not only lost its way in foreign trade, but the supply of coarse grains has also been greatly affected. In particular, the oil bean market has been manipulated, with prices lowered for dumping and held high for control. Moreover, in recent years, various countries have engaged in the construction of food security, storing as much as possible food grains such as rice, wheat, and oil beans. The continuous increase in prices is largely due to this.

The above three points cannot help but evoke some mixed feelings. We believe that although it is not necessary to hastily prohibit exports, the huge amount of japonica rice and thin rice being shipped to Tianjin, Qingdao, and other places this year is probably unprecedented. If it is for the consumption of the people in the north, that goes without saying. But if there is another purpose, it is difficult to guarantee that the rice and grains will not be smuggled in the most active smuggling areas, which is worthy of attention. As for the rise in flour and wheat prices, even if it is because the local wheat is insufficient and foreign wheat is needed to make up for it, and foreign wheat is not suitable for ordering due to import duties, a solution should be sought immediately, and inaction should not be tolerated. Otherwise, if the speculative effect is greater than the relationship of raw materials, the exchange should be supervised by the government and cracked down on to prevent it from harming the people's food. Furthermore, in terms of general food grains, there have been reports of drought and famine from the autumn of this year. We cannot be blindly optimistic because of this year's bumper harvest. We must know that in the current situation without statistical surveys, a major food shortage next year is very likely. We should be aware that in today's situation, the construction of food security is urgent. The outflow and inflow of food grains should be subject to appropriate management, and the adjustment of food grains, whether in peacetime or wartime, should be planned in a coordinated manner. In short, food policy is a whole and consistent one, and there must be a central executive agency to grasp its key points and determine appropriate plans based on major interests. If only piecemeal efforts are made, not only will disputes easily arise, but it will also be harmful to the people's food problems in the future.

British Constitution Faces Crisis: Cabinet Offers Final Advice, Parliamentarians Support Prime Minister, Rumors Swirl of King's Determination to Abdicate, Succession Becomes Problem

(London) Regarding the constitutional dispute caused by the marriage issue, it is widely rumored in Parliament that the King's confidants have sought the opinions of a majority of members. Political observers have recently declared that, regarding this dispute, members, whether belonging to the trade union or the Labor Party, cannot support the King, as their views seem to have converged, namely, that the Constitution stipulates that the King must abide by it. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

(London) Well-informed sources recently declared that the King invited his brothers, the Duke of York and the Duke of Kent, Prime Minister Baldwin, and other important figures to dinner at Fort Belvedere last night and, after lengthy discussions, has decided to abdicate. However, whether the successor to the throne will be his brother, the Duke of York, or Princess Elizabeth, daughter of the Duke of York, with Queen Mary and others forming a regency council to act on her behalf until she comes of age, has not yet been decided. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

(London) An Associated Press reporter learned today from reliable sources that King Edward has decided to abdicate rather than abandon the American woman Mrs. Simpson. This determination is said to be irreversible and may be announced to the House of Commons today. Prime Minister Baldwin met with the King at Fort Belvedere for five hours last night and, with the King's decision, hurriedly returned to his Downing Street residence early this morning to consult with Home Secretary Sir John Simon and scheduled an emergency cabinet meeting for 11:00 this morning to report to all cabinet members. The Duke of York, the Duke of Kent, and Monkton, legal advisor to the Duchy of Cornwall, were present at last night's meeting in the palace. People in Buckingham Palace now firmly believe that the situation is about to take a sharp turn. (National Telegram, 9th)

(London) A political reporter for the Mail declared today that political figures generally believe that King Edward may ultimately feel compelled to abdicate. Various preparations are already being made. Financial figures have also learned that the King has conveyed his intention to abdicate to Prime Minister Baldwin. (National Telegram, 9th)

Cabinet Meeting: Tight Security, Details Unknown

(London) The Cabinet met at 11:00 this morning to discuss the constitutional dispute caused by the King's marriage issue. Security was very tight, and the details are unknown. It is only known that Prime Minister Baldwin does not intend to make a statement to the House of Commons today. (National Telegram, 9th)

(London) At the regular cabinet meeting held at 11:00 this morning, the constitutional dispute involving the King's marriage was the main issue. All cabinet members attended and deliberated in secret for two and a half hours. An hour before the meeting, Home Secretary Simon went to the Prime Minister's residence on Downing Street. Shortly after, Mr. Monkton, the private secretary of the Duke of York, also arrived. Sir Peacock, the Receiver-General of the Duchy of Cornwall, also arrived at the Prime Minister's residence this morning. The King's brothers, the Duke of York and the Duke of Kent, left the King's residence, Fort Belvedere, together at 11:00 last night, but the Duke of Kent returned to the palace at 1:00 this morning and spent the night there. Mr. Monkton also stayed overnight at the palace. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

Fort Belvedere: Meetings Until Late at Night, Prime Minister and Other Important Figures Dine at Palace, Wedding Issue Under Last Consideration

(London) Last night, Prime Minister Baldwin had dinner at Fort Belvedere with the King, the Duke of York, the Archbishop of Canterbury, Lord Monckton, Legal Advisor to the Duchy of Cornwall, and Mr. Meville, Private Secretary to the Duke of York, and held important discussions on the constitutional crisis. The Prime Minister arrived at the palace at 5:30 PM with Mr. Monckton and Mr. Melville. The Duke of Kent had been with the King all day and was already at the palace. The Duke of York's car entered through the back door of the palace at 6:30 PM, but the occupant of the car could not be identified. The Prime Minister stayed at the palace for four hours and forty-five minutes, leaving at 10:15 PM and returning to his residence on Downing Street. Home Secretary Simon had arrived at the residence at 9:30 PM to await him. The Prime Minister did not arrive until 11:00 PM and talked with Simon for forty-five minutes before he left. When the House of Commons meets today, there will be no detailed announcement of the situation, but it may be briefly mentioned. When the Cabinet holds a regular meeting at 11:00 this morning, it will still discuss the King's marriage. Yesterday, activity was not only taking place at Fort Belvedere, but also at Whitehall (where various government departments are located), Westminster Abbey, and Buckingham Palace, all of which were unusually busy. The King's private secretary, Major Hardinge, traveled by car from Lambeth Palace to Buckingham Palace last night to see Archbishop of Canterbury Cosmo Gordon Lang. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

(London) Based on the current situation, the outcome of the palace meeting does not seem to have resulted in any decision, and the parties involved are still maintaining their original positions. As for how the dispute will ultimately end, opinions vary. The Cabinet still believes that the King's abdication is inevitable, while those around the King say that the points of contention are not insurmountable. Another group of people believe that no decision can be made until Mrs. Simpson's legal advisor, Mr. Goddard, and the famous London doctor, Dr. Kirkwood, return to London, as the three have flown to Cannes, France, yesterday. However, political figures generally believe that the dispute must be resolved quickly, as the current situation is protracted and could endanger the political situation. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

British House of Commons Meets, Labor MPs Ask Questions, Prime Minister Will Continue to Make Statements Today and Tomorrow, Political Circles Expect Abdication Is Almost Inevitable

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin made no statement in the House of Commons today regarding the constitutional dispute, but said he hoped to have something to announce tomorrow. When the House of Commons reconvened this afternoon, Labor opposition leader Clement Attlee asked Baldwin if he could add anything to Monday's official statement. Baldwin replied, "I have nothing to announce today, but I hope to have a statement tomorrow." Labor MP Mr. Paling then spoke, asking the government to pay attention to the fact that the lack of a decision on the constitutional dispute has caused great inconvenience in the financial sector, and asked the Prime Minister to advise the King to make a decision quickly. Baldwin replied that he had paid attention to this situation. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

(London) Political figures and members of Parliament all believe that the King's abdication is almost inevitable, and may become a reality within hours after last night's meeting at Fort Belvedere. After the King abdicates, he may be renamed the Earl of Chester. People in the Parliament's tearoom said that several legal advisors to the Crown were very busy making contacts today, and what they were discussing was the issue of the King's financial resources after his abdication. It is noted that the British Parliament passed the Act of Settlement in 1701, which stipulates that the British throne cannot be vacated except upon the death of the monarch or by law passed by Parliament. Therefore, in legal principle, it cannot be vacant. Generally speaking, after Edward VIII decides to abdicate, he should send an edict to Parliament publicly announcing his intention to abdicate, and then Parliament will pass a law to accept it and announce who will be established as the new monarch. In short, until the parliaments of the United Kingdom and its dominions formally announce the accession of the new monarch, Edward VIII will still reign over the country for one more day. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

Canberra. The Australian House of Representatives met for eighteen minutes today before adjourning. Prime Minister Lyons said, "I sincerely hope that this crisis can be avoided, so it is best for Parliament to remain silent." Labor MPs opposed the adjournment due to a lack of opportunity to express their views. Leader Curtin believed that the King should have the freedom to choose his marriage, "but the King must also bear the full responsibility for his personal conscience and the entire empire. Once the choice is made, the Labor Party hopes that the King will not abdicate." (National Telegram, 8th)

(London) It was learned today from responsible sources here that the Parliament of the Irish Free State may prevent the abdication of the British King by "joking." The parliament may refuse to pass the necessary legislation under the Statute of Westminster to prevent the Duke of York from ascending the throne. It is declared here that confidants of Free State President Éamon de Valera have issued this warning to the authorities in London. (National Telegram, 8th)

Inside Story of Mysterious Plane Revealed: Mrs. Simpson's Legal Advisor and Famous Doctor Travel Together, How Can the King's Lovers Force a Smile When Their Hearts Are Full of Worries?

Cannes, France. London suburb of Croydon Aerodrome. A mysterious plane flew out yesterday morning and arrived in Marseille in the afternoon. The plane carried three people: besides Mrs. Simpson's legal advisor, Mr. Goddard, the other two were a famous London doctor, Dr. Kirkwood, and Mr. Barron, a clerk of Mr. Goddard's law firm. After landing in Marseille, the three transferred to a car and arrived here that evening, staying at a hotel. According to Lord Brownlow, the King's private secretary, Dr. Kirkwood is a friend of Mr. Goddard, who is slightly ill and fears that his condition will worsen due to the hardship of the journey, so he came with the doctor. Dr. Kirkwood is now scheduled to move to Monte Carlo today. When Lord Brownlow spoke, he looked overwhelmed with grief. (Havas dispatch, 9th)

Cannes, France. London suburb of Croydon Aerodrome. A mysterious plane carrying three passengers flew out this morning and arrived in Marseille at 4:15 PM. The names of the three passengers were kept secret when they departed and have now been revealed (see previous dispatch). After landing in Marseille, the three had a quick meal and then continued on their way to this place. According to two statements made to the press by Lord Brownlow, the King's private secretary, Mrs. Simpson does not intend to return to England anytime soon, and her residence in London should be closed urgently. Mr. Goddard came here to discuss this issue with Mrs. Simpson. As for Mrs. Simpson's plans, she intends to stay here until Christmas, after which her destination is unknown. Also, since Mrs. Simpson arrived here, the Villa Lou Viei has been heavily guarded, and journalists and photographers have been lingering outside the gates all day and are not allowed to enter. Today, one British and one American photographer from each country were allowed to enter to meet with Mrs. Simpson. Mrs. Simpson looked worried. One of them asked Mrs. Simpson to smile so that he could take a photo. Mrs. Simpson angrily replied, "Why should I smile? Do you think this is a time for me to smile?" Soon after, several local photographers were also allowed to enter to take several photos of Mrs. Simpson. At this point, Lord Brownlow said that Mrs. Simpson had satisfied the journalists and now wished to stay quiet and rest, and asked them not to bother her anymore. As for Mrs. Simpson's health, she is currently in good health and has not consulted a doctor. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

(Rome) Rumors spread that Mrs. Simpson will come here and stay at the villa of British Lord Beresford. The caretakers of the villa are unaware of this, but the police here will take various measures to protect her. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

British Press Commentary: Mrs. Simpson's Statement Is Enough to Save the Crisis

(London) An editorial in The Times said that the King had proposed a course of action, but others had advised him against it based on the Constitution. We dare to assert that the King will accept this advice. According to the provisions of the British Constitution, when the King, the Cabinet, and Parliament reach an impasse, and there are doubts about public opinion backing the Cabinet and Parliament, they may appeal to the people of the country. However, this provision does not apply to today's events, and the King has no such doubts. Therefore, the plan for a morganatic marriage has been abandoned. What the King is now considering is whether to take any other form of action. The duty of the Cabinet is to give the King all the information they know when he consults them, so that the King has a complete understanding of the consequences of the course of action he chooses. It is not permissible for the Cabinet to directly or indirectly advise the King to make other plans, and the Cabinet has never done so. The Daily Mail said that Mrs. Simpson's statement that she was willing to avoid any action or suggestion that would harm the King or the throne has changed the whole situation. This serious and disturbing crisis now has hope of ending soon. Mrs. Simpson's actions make it possible for the King to continue in his position and save the country from the sorrow that would be caused by the King's abdication. The Daily Express said that we can rejoice now. The crisis has become history. The King is still above us. The issue of the King trampling on the Cabinet and the Cabinet forcing the King to submit in matters concerning the King himself has not arisen. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

Japanese Thinker Baba Criticizes German-Japanese Agreement, Feels Emotional About Anglo-Japanese Alliance Now and Then, Foreign Minister Arita Has Made Efforts to Ease Public Opinion

(Tokyo) Prominent Japanese liberal thinker Baba declared that the news of the German-Japanese agreement was a bolt from the blue for the Japanese people. He solemnly stated that in 1902, the whole country was pleased with the establishment of the Anglo-Japanese Alliance, but this time, the feeling towards the German-Japanese agreement is one of deep anxiety. If the sole purpose of the German-Japanese agreement is to oppose communism, then this kind of action cannot be considered wrong. However, since the conclusion of this agreement, other countries in the world have the impression that Japan has become a fascist country. In other words, Japan's ideology is neither fascist nor communist. Japan is willing to maintain a middle course and complete a constitutional government situated between the two extremes mentioned above. Judging from the current situation, Japan seems to have lost its neutral friends, such as the United Kingdom and the United States, and is seeking friendship with Italy and Germany. The Hirota Cabinet's recent secret diplomacy, such as the German-Japanese and Italian-Japanese agreements, has not only caused unrest in domestic political circles, but also aroused the attention of democratic countries overseas. People generally believe that the establishment of the two agreements was due to pressure from the military, or there is considerable reason. The Hirota Cabinet is very sensitive to the domestic and foreign reactions. Recently, the police have often suddenly sent people to visit the leaders of foreign commercial firms in Yokohama to ask for their opinions on the German-Japanese agreement, etc. In order to ease overseas public opinion, Foreign Minister Arita recently hosted foreign reporters in Tokyo and answered questions about the anti-communist agreement for more than an hour without showing any signs of fatigue. Finally, a foreign reporter asked, "If the Communist Party tries to subvert the Nanjing government, will Japan help Nanjing to prevent it from being overthrown?" The Japanese Foreign Minister replied that this question was outside the scope of the anti-communist agreement and could not be answered. (Reuters dispatch, 9th) The Splendor of Buckingham Palace in England.

Western Rebels Actively Reinforcing: General Offensive Imminent, Bombardment of Madrid Has Not Stopped All Night, 60,000 International Volunteers Assist in Battle

Madrid. At dawn today, a large contingent of fresh troops from the Spanish Nationalist Army arrived at the front line, indicating that the Nationalist Army's general offensive is indeed imminent. Last night, the city was bombarded by Nationalist artillery fire, which continued all night. This is also the prelude to the general offensive. The Nationalist artillery fire was aimed at the northwest of the capital. In the past few days, the Nationalist Army has transported 29 military supplies and 40 new aircraft. The government forces are now stepping up the excavation of trenches and the erection of barbed wire to prepare for resistance. International Drug Trafficking Case: Warmary, Ailing, Subjected to Trial; American Court Finds Guilty, Sentencing Scheduled for This Friday

Los Angeles: Ms. Warmary, a Chinese-European mixed-race woman who was arrested in the United States last month for drug trafficking, is said to be involved with a large-scale drug smuggling organization on the West Coast of the United States. The Federal Court opened a trial today and is scheduled to announce the verdict on Friday. According to U.S. law, the maximum penalty for the aforementioned charge is 20 years imprisonment and a $10,000 fine. (Reuters, 9th)

Los Angeles: Warmary, a Eurasian woman from Shanghai, has been found guilty by a federal jury here of smuggling drugs worth $100,000 into the United States. The woman's lawyer defended her, saying she was used by a large-scale smuggling organization but was exposed due to her incompetence in smuggling. According to reports, the case was cracked in mid-August this year. At that time, a Japanese ship came from the Far East to St. Peter. Federal agents boarded the ship to search for drugs and wanted to detain Warmary. The woman resisted desperately. Then the agents cut open the woman's suitcase with a knife, and there were as many as 54 pounds of heroin hidden in sixteen compartments. The woman then lowered her head and was speechless, and later agreed to confess the mastermind of the smuggling organization, because she claimed that she was just a poorly compensated tool. After receiving the drugs in Shanghai each time, she crossed to the United States and handed them over to a Polish man named Branstad, who was well-known in Shanghai. It is said that this person had already gone to the United States at that time. According to the confession, the anti-smuggling authorities placed the woman in a hotel here to attract accomplices. The woman used a trick to escape, took a plane to New York, boarded a German ship, and was about to sail to Europe, but was still arrested by agents. On the ship, the woman tried to jump into the port to commit suicide, but was also unsuccessful. At the same time, after investigations by both the United States and Shanghai, it was known that the Polish man, Branstad, provided by Warmary was not entirely accurate. Although Branstad had left Shanghai at that time, he had not yet arrived in the United States, because he detoured through Rome and Barcelona to Cuba, and then flew to Mexico, intending to enter the United States from the southern border to meet Warmary, but was sent back to Cuba by the Mexican authorities. According to reports from the local police station, the Cuban bureau also did not accept him, so he went to New York. Presumably, he had learned of Warmary's arrest on the way, so he did not arrive in New York and hanged himself. Therefore, the New York Federal agents only obtained Branstad's body. Later, Warmary continued to confess that she and Branstad were both hired by a man named Stie, who was formerly an accountant at the Shanghai Baolong Hospital, and all the smuggling plans were directed by him. When Shanghai wanted to arrest Stie, Stie had disappeared. However, several weeks later, he was found in a vacant lot in the French Concession of Shanghai, unconscious from poisoning, and died the next day without saying a word. It is still unknown whether Stie was also a tool. The date of the trial of Warmary's case has been postponed several times, once because the woman was ill, and once because the defense lawyer went elsewhere, and only arrived in court last week to be tried. However, the woman was still unable to walk due to illness, and was brought from the prison hospital to the court in a sedan chair. Shortly after the trial began, the woman fainted, so the trial was postponed again to this week. The judge's verdict has not yet been announced today. (National News Agency, 8th)

Under Certain Party's Instigation, Bandit Puppets in Chahar Provoking Trouble, Imminent Invasion; Certain Party's Regular Army Stationed in Northern Chahar, Wang Ying Indeed Under House Arrest in Shangdu

Zhang HaiPeng's puppet troops, numbering 3,000, had completed their concentration in Battai, northeast of Taolin, on the 6th and are also preparing to participate in the westward invasion. Quantity of Bandit Puppet Military Supplies Transported

Guangdong Construction Bureau Director Liu Weichi Discusses Guangdong Province Construction: Adjusting Guangdong's Grain Supply with Surplus Grain from Neighboring Provinces; Private Citizens Can Undertake the Operation of Province-Run Factories; Silk Industry Loan Plan Specifies Three Steps

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since Liu Weichi became the head of the Construction Bureau of Guangdong Province, he has been very proactive in planning and implementing construction projects. Recently, according to Mr. Liu's detailed account of the latest progress in the construction undertakings of Guangdong Province, the details are recorded as follows:

Relief of Grain Supply

The grain supply in this province is quite scarce, coupled with a poor late harvest this year. After the four provinces of Guangdong, Hunan, Jiangxi, and Anhui jointly proposed economic cooperation, the grain that this province lacks will be addressed by organizing a grain transport company to transport surplus grain from various provinces. Because the measures for selling Hunan rice in Guangdong have not yet been finalized, it is proposed to start with Jiangxi first. However, this matter still needs to be considered. Originally, using the surplus from other provinces to supplement the shortage in this province is an excellent idea. Moreover, abundant harvests are related to weather conditions. Although this province has experienced a poor harvest this year, neighboring provinces have had good harvests. Mutual assistance is the only way to adjust and enrich the grain supply. However, recently, some people have advocated reducing the import tax on foreign rice to allow sufficient foreign rice to enter the market for adjustment purposes. However, I still believe that transporting rice from neighboring provinces to Guangdong for relief is a better option. Before these two methods are finalized, the grain problem in this province still needs to be discussed and there is no thorough solution yet.

Inviting Private Operation of Province-Run Factories

Regarding the private operation of province-run factories, this idea is indeed under consideration. For industries operated by the government, if it is deemed that merchants have the ability to handle them, it is more appropriate for merchants to operate them. However, larger-scale projects must be undertaken by the government. The factories recently established by the government do not offer any particular advantages because it has now been decided that both public and private factories must pay all kinds of taxes equally. Moreover, existing merchants are quite willing to take over. Previously, the responsibility for the operation and equipment of various province-run factories rested with the Construction Bureau. Now, the Construction Bureau has established a General Management Office and a Supervisory Committee for province-run industries. In the future, the development plans for factories and the procurement of raw materials will be handled by these two organizations. After these two organizations complete the procedures, they will submit them to the provincial government for discussion at the provincial affairs meeting. After multiple procedures and designs by various organizations, the question becomes whether the equipment of the province-run factories will be suitable and thorough. It is not just a matter of setting up responsibilities. For all undertakings, finance and economics must support each other. Finance should consider economics, and economics should also consider finance. They cannot be discussed separately. In short, I believe that province-run factories that private citizens are capable of operating should still be handed over to private citizens for operation. The government can reduce the preparation of a large amount of working capital, and the national economy can develop.

Developing Qiongya

Regarding the development of Qiongya's industry, the government currently does not have definite capital, so it now advocates encouraging private investment. The government has decided to start with facilitating transportation for the development of Qiongya's development plan. The Qiongya Island highway has already been completed, but due to a lack of funding, the bridge equipment has not yet been constructed. According to the budget, building with cement would require 700,000 to 800,000 yuan, while using fir wood would require more than 100,000 yuan. In addition to allocating funds from the road construction budget, the rest is still being raised. In the future, it will be repaid from the profits of the transport plan. As for the future development plan for Qiongya transportation, in addition to ordering the Qiongya Highway Traffic Management Office to step up its work, there are also plans to build seaports and large docks to facilitate the berthing of ships. In addition, there are also plans to build railways or wide highways to connect with all sides. Chairman Song's recent trip to Qiong also decided to imitate and implement the Qiongya development plan. He is now going to inspect it in order to implement it. As for the Xisha and Nansha Islands, which are rich in seaweed, they have long been coveted by foreigners who often steal them. The government has designed preventive measures to prevent resources from being taken away.

Water and Steel Plants

The Weng River Hydropower Plant was previously designed by the authorities, but due to the huge scale of the project and the large amount of funding required, construction has not yet begun. If the power plant is completed in the future, it will be able to thoroughly solve problems such as rural water conservancy. I believe that even if foreign capital is used to handle it when the government is temporarily unable to do so, it is still acceptable. The total cost requires more than 50 million yuan, which the government cannot afford for the time being. Regarding the progress of the steel plant, it has been decided to start with technical and financial aspects first. After technician He from this bureau went to Beijing for instructions, it was decided that this province should continue to handle it, and the central authorities will provide appropriate subsidies, and so on.

Silk Industry Loans

In order to revitalize the rural economy, Liu Weichi, in order to save the silk industry in Guangdong Province, specially planned silk industry loans with the Provincial Bank and the Bank of Communications. After several consultations and dispatching personnel to various villages to investigate, Liao Chongzhen, Director of the Silk Improvement Bureau of the Construction Bureau, put forward opinions for the reference of the Provincial and Jiaotong Bank authorities. At present, the negotiations have been generally completed and will be implemented as soon as they are approved. The loan plan is divided into three parts, which will be carried out in sequence. The methods are roughly as follows: The first step is to launch yarn and silk weaving loans. The method is to first select the Lunzhen area, which already has sound cooperatives, for a pilot project. If it is effective, it will be promoted to the silk weaving concentrated areas such as Minle, Shajiao, and Huanglian for a pilot project. The steps are divided into two phases: (1) First, grant loans to existing cooperatives for transportation and sales, and production credit loans, so that they can expand their organization and increase services, and call on more than 400 weaving households in Lunzhen (about 2,600 looms) to join the cooperative, run their own drying yards, so that they can dry black viscose yarn and silk by themselves (that is, self-made finished products), and organize their own sales departments to directly connect with sales in Shanghai, Nanyang and other places. (2) After Lunzhen has been successfully handled, gradually promote it to Minle, Shajiao, Huanglian and other places, and use loans to reward weaving households to improve existing machinery and technology, and manufacture new products obtained from the regional research institutes of the silk industry in Lunzhen and Minle. In accordance with the previous method, the finished products are graded and directly transported to other ports, so that they can meet the needs of the times, in order to seek the survival and development of the Guangdong yarn and silk weaving industry. The second step is to launch machinery silk reeling industry loans. The method is also divided into two phases: (1) Unite existing silk factories to organize a cooperative foreign trade agency. Each silk factory is a member of the cooperative foreign trade agency, reeling the same grade of raw silk and unifying direct foreign trade. Before the products of each factory reach the purchase period, the bank will allow the mortgage of its raw silk or factory properties, and provide financial accommodation to facilitate turnover. (2) United cooperation with the foreign trade agency members, all factory reconstruction, and installation of new machinery, procurement of improved raw materials, and manufacturing of high-grade raw silk, still according to the previous method to unify the product grade and common foreign trade. The reconstruction costs of its factory machinery, etc., are loaned by the banking industry for 70%, and the remaining 30% is raised by the members themselves, or requested by the government for subsidies. The rent obtained by the factory should be used to pay off the principal and interest of the banking industry in installments in advance. Before it is paid off, the factory will be used as a guarantee for the banking industry's 70% investment. The third step is to launch seed production and silkworm raising industry cooperative loans. The method is that the silkworm improvement area and the banking industry will jointly promote the establishment of the cooperative. The former is responsible for technical improvement and organizational guidance, and the latter is responsible for the audit of accounts. Each member of the cooperative should provide mutual guarantees, so that credit production loans can be carried out, and all products of the members will be handed over to the cooperative for joint transportation and sales. As for the silkworm raising cooperative, it should also establish close contact with the silk reeling factory in order to reduce the exploitation of middlemen.

Active Municipal Facilities in the Capital: Feces Management and Expansion of the Municipal Railway

Nanjing Communication: The Municipal Government held a memorial week for the Prime Minister at 8:00 a.m. on the first day of this week. All staff members were present, chaired by Secretary-General Wang Shufang. After leading the ceremony, Councilor Zhang Jianming reported on three matters handled and participated in by basic staff: (1) Regarding the first membership solicitation of the Municipal Air Defense Association, it was briefly stated that since the Municipal Air Defense Association held the first membership solicitation meeting on September 15, a total of more than 880 teams have been established by the end of November. The number of members solicited this time was originally set at 100,000, including all sectors of the Party, government, military, police, and academia. Ordinary members are limited to citizens who have received training, so the initial handling felt very simple. However, later, many citizens automatically requested to join, and the number of natural members from all sectors was more than the original number of 100,000. Therefore, as a result, the association issued eight registration books and more than 100,000 copies. About 80,000 people have officially joined after paying their membership fees, which proves that the citizens of this city have a considerable understanding of the importance of air defense, which is worthy of our attention. (2) Regarding the management of feces in this city, it was briefly stated that since the Feces Management Office of this city was officially opened on July 5, it was first tried out in the third and fifth districts, and improved from time to time. Initially, it was stipulated that feces collectors should collect feces from house to house, transport them to the various feces boat docks on the Qinhuai River, load them into feces boats and transport them to Shuixi Gate, and use feces pumps to pump them out of the city and hand them over to merchants for sale. According to the statistics, there are more than 50,000 households in the third and fifth districts, but only more than 8,000 households collect feces in accordance with the regulations by feces collectors, accounting for only one-sixth of the total. The reasons are that a very small number of households use flush toilets and do not need feces collectors to collect feces, and a small number of households have vegetable gardens for their own use, or have septic tank equipment to dispose of them by themselves. Most households, either because they are close to the toilet, or because they are poor, want to save costs and secretly dump and wash them. Now, in order to unify management, the Feces Management Office has specially formulated rules for tidying up and managing toilets, and announced and implemented them, registering all toilets in the city, and absolutely prohibiting the dumping and washing of toilets in the toilets, because without such measures, the feces problem in this city cannot be uniformly controlled, and there is no possibility of thorough improvement. As for the various feces boat docks on the Qinhuai River in the city, which citizens have complained about, if they are all canceled and docks are set up on the moat outside the city, it will be possible to implement them soon. In short, the feces management in this city is still in the early stages, and it is hoped that citizens will do their best to assist in order to achieve perfection. If you have any opinions, please also give more instructions to the organizers of the office, so that they can adopt and implement them. (3) Regarding the expansion of the municipal railway, it was briefly stated that the expansion project of the municipal railway has now been completed. The situation has been reported to you before. Recently, the negotiation of joint transportation with the Jiangnan Railway Company has been generally agreed upon and will be implemented soon. The municipal railway has now been opened to Jiankang Road, and will be opened to Wudingmen next week. In the future, after the joint transportation with the Jiangnan Railway, it can directly reach Sunjiabu in Anhui. As for the joint transportation with the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, the mayor sent a letter to the Ministry of Railways and proposed four methods: 1. The Beijing Railway will set up a track at Jinchuan Gate to connect with the municipal railway. 2. The railway department and the municipal government will cooperate in the Central Street Station of the municipal railway. 3. The Central Street Station of the municipal railway will be the central station to accommodate vehicles from all aspects entering the city. The railway department and the municipal government will jointly manage it. 4. The railway department will try various methods to make full use of the municipal railway. Recently, a reply letter from the Ministry of Railways was received, expressing its agreement to the principle of making full use of the municipal railway. Regarding the expansion of the municipal railway and the Central Street Station, it is hoped that the municipal government will operate and manage it alone. Regarding the connection between the Beijing-Shanghai Railway at Jinchuan Gate and the municipal railway, it is argued that the connection with the municipal railway should still be at Xiaguan Station. The reason is that if the connection is made at Jinchuan Gate, the timetable must be rearranged, which is very inconvenient, and Xiaguan Station already has very perfect facilities, which is easy to do. Regarding this point, our research results show that there is no major relationship between the connection of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway at Jinchuan Gate or Xiaguan with the municipal railway. However, it will take 20 more minutes to transfer to the municipal railway at Xiaguan. According to the actual situation, except for a very small number of passengers who get off at Hepingmen because they have their own cars to save time and avoid noise, most people will be happy to use the train if it can drive into the city. Therefore, this fact is not a problem. Now, the municipal government intends to actively reorganize the old road section of the municipal railway, such as replacing sleepers, replacing steel rails, repairing bridges, and repairing houses at Xiaguan and Central Street stations, so that it can realize traffic with the Beijing-Shanghai Railway as soon as possible to benefit the citizens.

Suzhou

Police Officer's Jealousy and Murder Case

Yang Chunyi, a policeman in the First Squadron of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, from Bengbu, Anhui, had been living with a woman named Shen Cuie. In July last year, Shen Cuie abandoned the old and changed to the new, and lived with Zhang Longhai. Because of being lovelorn, Yang tried to commit suicide with a pistol but failed. On July 15 of the same year, he took a fake leave from the team, carried a box gun, and went to Zhang Hailong's house at No. 131 Hetan Pavilion Road, Jiangwan Town, and shot Zhang Hailong and his mistress Shen Cuie to death, and injured Shen Cuie's sister Shen Xiaomei. Later, he abandoned his uniform and box gun in Tongle Lane, Hongkou, and fled without a trace. In September of this year, Yang Chunyi wrote a letter from Bengbu, Anhui, to Shen Xiaomei, expressing his apology and asking that the past be spared from prosecution. After receiving the letter, Shen Xiaomei reported to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and notified the Bengbu Public Security Bureau of Anhui to arrest Yang and send him to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for transfer to the Shanghai Local Court for trial. He was sentenced to life imprisonment for the crime of murder. The prosecutor believed that Yang Chunyi continuously premeditated murder, and the sentence was too light, so he appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. The Second Criminal Court held a hearing yesterday afternoon, and Shen Xiaomei also appeared in court and appointed lawyer Zhuang Pengnian to defend Yang. As a result, the sentence will be announced on the 14th of this month.

Wuxi

Meat Merchants Request Exemption from Business Tax

The Business Tax Collection Bureau of this county believes that the sale of fresh meat by meat merchants, or the production and sale of cooked meat, is obviously another business activity and should be subject to business tax in accordance with the regulations. However, the meat industry believes that the slaughter of pigs is entirely self-slaughtered and self-sold, and is not purchased from others, which seems to be different from the general situation of so-called concurrent operation. Therefore, it sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it forward a letter to the Business Tax Bureau to exempt it from collection in order to relieve merchants' difficulties. After receiving the letter, the Chamber of Commerce stated that since the meat industry in Wuxi is self-slaughtered and self-sold, it is difficult to say that it is another business activity. If it is said that taxes are being collected, officials and merchants specially sent a letter to the Tax Bureau, requesting that from January next year, the method of Zhao Wu County be followed to assess and collect taxes from larger cooked meat stores, and also asked them to consider the difficulties of merchants and not to be harsh.

Printing Workers Strike

The accounting book printing company of Pan Jinfeng in Jiangyin Lane outside the North Gate of this county is opened by Tao Wenbing. There are more than 10 workers. However, Tao is usually harsh to people. Recently, the working hours have reached 17 hours, and the internal wages are uneven, which has caused dissatisfaction among the workers, who believe that it violates the printing regulations. Therefore, each worker submitted four requests to the owner, and after receiving no satisfactory answer, they went on strike on the 5th of this month, and requested relief from the Printing Industry Association. After the association mediated between labor and management, there was no result, and the situation became deadlocked. On the 9th, all the workers of the office petitioned the Party and government authorities for relief. However, if this case is not resolved early, it is feared that it will affect the overall situation of the printing industry in the county.

Nantong

Cotton Firms Stop Weighing Due to Losses

Cotton in Tong County has had a bumper harvest this year. Due to the competition among cotton merchants, the market price has soared, sometimes even higher than Shanghai. Most of the cotton transported to Shanghai and Wuxi has been lost. Various firms once jointly raised the weighing scale to suppress the rise in price. However, cotton farmers, unable to obtain high prices, have stored the cotton in the farmers' warehouses, waiting for a good price in the coming spring. At the moment, the goods arriving in the villages are scarce, and the firms do not dare to accept cotton during the period of low prices and high prices. They have stopped weighing and collecting cotton.

Bengbu

Continuing to Reorganize Anfeng Pond

Anfeng Pond in Shouxian County, northern Anhui, also known as Shao Pond, was created by Sun Shu'ao, the Chu prime minister in the Spring and Autumn Period. It is a famous water conservancy area since ancient times. Its management is actually earlier than the Northwest Qin Canal, Han Canal, Zheng Canal, and Bai Canal. Initially, it irrigated 1 million mu of land, or 400,000 mu, and gradually fell into disuse over time. Now only more than 100,000 mu of irrigated area remain. Its water source is one to draw water from the Pi River, and the other is to receive mountain water. Later, because the path of the Pi River was blocked, the irrigated area shrank day by day. The Anhui Provincial Government plans to restore the old state. After sending personnel to survey and design the reorganization, the construction methods are: A. Dredge the bottom of the canal for drawing the Pi River to half a meter below the dry water level, with a width of two meters, and extend the original spillway dam. A total of 121,231 yuan is required for four types of construction costs. Type B requires 61,043 yuan. The provincial government adopted four types of methods and allocated funds to build it last year. The first phase of earthwork engineering was organized by the Huai River Guidance Committee. The second phase of the project has been transferred from the Huai River Guidance Committee to the Provincial Government for organization. Ma Jidi, the magistrate of Shouxian County, believes that although the dredging project of the Pi River source has been completed, the intake culvert and the repair of the pond and river embankment must be continued to promote irrigation effectiveness. He specially telegraphed the Construction Department a few days ago, asking for personnel to be sent to preside over the construction. The Construction Department replied by telegram, stating that the soil and rock engineering for the Anfeng Pond pond embankment and river embankment had previously been approved by the Huai River Guidance Committee, and the Water Conservancy Engineering Department was ordered to handle it. According to the construction methods proposed by the department, the Huai River Guidance Committee was transferred to allocate funds for the case. It is now waiting for the funds to arrive for construction. It is now heard that before the construction starts, the Anfeng Pond Pond Construction Committee has been ordered to reorganize to facilitate the project.

Hangzhou

Continuing to Build Yongrui Ping Road

Yongrui Ping Highway is an important transportation route from Wenzhou directly to the provincial capital. Construction began as early as last year, but it was suspended halfway due to financial difficulties. The Construction Department now believes that the earthwork of the road has been completed, and in order to continue the project, it has specially approved the central government to allocate 100,000 yuan for engineering expenses. The remaining 300,000 yuan will be raised by the province itself. All bridge and road surface projects have been contracted to merchants and will be built soon. It is expected to be completed and opened to traffic in February next year.

Grain: Rumors of Foreign Wheat Being Ordered; Wheat Flour Once Slightly Declined

After the wheat market opened in the morning, it saw a sharp drop at one point. The quoted prices for foreign wheat were: Chicago down 1/4 to 1/10 of a cent, Canada down 2/10 of a cent. The market rumors of foreign wheat being ordered have been confirmed. It is said that two ships have been ordered at a price of $9.42. With this news, people's hearts became greatly worried. The December price fell by 14/100 of a cent, and the January to March prices also fell by about 1/10 of a cent. Although the market sentiment was loose, the speculative atmosphere was strong. Therefore, it immediately rebounded by 3-5/100 of a cent. Approaching the afternoon opening, it rose due to active buying from outside the industry, and the flour market also showed signs of rebounding. Therefore, the prices of each month rose steadily, only slightly lower than the previous closing price by 1-5/100 of a cent. This situation seems to imply an uncertain future and a difficult immediate loosening. The current wheat prices are still firm. The opening prices for wheat from various places are: Kaiyang He Yaowan wheat at $6.65, Hefei wheat at $6.54, Shaoxing wheat at $6.45 and $6.38 for the second grade, Dongtai wheat at $6.50, Daorenqiao wheat at $6.37, and Pudong wheat at $5.75 and $5.77 for the second grade. Rice Boats Detained Are Gradually Released; River Rice Arrivals Surge

35,000 Piculs of Rice Arrive in Southern Shanghai; Sales Are Brisk in Local Streets and Northern Areas; Arrival of Ke Xian Rice Causes Market Prices to Remain Steady

Northern Shanghai: Rice boats detained for several days in the Jiwang Temple area were released the night before last. Yesterday morning, nearly a hundred arrived at the gate, with more arriving later, which calmed people's minds. Market prices immediately dropped by one or two cents. Later, because buyers heard that Southern Shanghai still had strong demand, selling prices were quite firm. However, due to the relentless demand for exports, prices were difficult to lower. As shops had low inventories, prices moved slightly lower, and various goods in the market were active. Except for white粳, which was slightly lower than the highest price, Bo Dao and Zao Dao were selling well, and market prices were strong. Yang Du Jian was stable, and Ke Jian was in demand. Prices of other goods were weak, falling by a few cents to a dime. In the future, the prices of various goods are expected to tighten.

Southern Shanghai: Yesterday, due to the gradual opening of the gate for ships from various gangs that had been blocked in the Neijiang River, a surge of arrivals reached a total of 160 to 170, with a total of 34,000 to 35,000 piculs of goods. Among them, Bo Dao still accounted for the majority, with about 110 to 120 ships. Fortunately, demand was also strong. The Pingjin Qingyan and other gangs handled 13,000 to 14,000 packages of Bo Dao and more than 5,000 packages of Hou Geng. Local street sales were also good, so there were not many left, and almost all were cleared. However, after this round of purchases, demand was somewhat saturated, so the market became sluggish. As a result, the prices of Hou and Bo Geng were all fixed. Due to the lack of supply of Du Yang Jian and Yin Bian Yuan, they showed a beautiful color again, but the prices varied.

Ke Xian: Yesterday, the market for Ke Xian rice saw continued strong demand in the local streets, with囤戶 (speculators) continuing to inquire. Demand from Henan remained active, so there was a need for market prices to continue to rise. However, there was a strong arrival of new rice at the Yangtze River head the day before yesterday, with more than 10,000 packages arriving daily. Also, rice detained in Jiading and other places was all released. Some local and foreign buyers stopped to wait and see. As cargo owners had both existing and arriving goods, they were willing to sell according to the market. Therefore, the rising trend stopped. A total of 4,647 packages of Gan rice, 945 packages of Xiang rice, 3,000 packages of Wen Xian, and 350 packages of Jiaxing rice were released, with prices similar to those of the previous market.

Piece Goods: Various Types of Woolen Cloth Are Very Popular

Shipments to Beijing, Hangzhou, and Other Places Are Very Strong; Business in Local Streets Is Also Brisk

Due to the cold weather recently, woolen cloth sales have been brisk. Sales in Nanjing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, and other places are particularly good. Men's and women's clothing stores, large and small, have been continuously adding a large number of配货 (goods to match outfits). Goods such as riding breeches, chocodings, crolets, meltons, plain thick woolens, medium-thick serge, black and gray hood woolens, various overcoat woolens, sleeve linings, etc., are all selling very well. Tianshun Shen Da Transport Company is shipping goods to Beijing, Hangzhou, and other places every day, which is quite crowded. Clothing shops on Xiaoximen Daxin Street, Sichuan Road, Avenue Joffre, and overcoat workshops in the Ji畝地 area all have strong purchasing appetites. Shoe and hat shops in the city and other places are also purchasing and cutting. The wholesale and retail business of woolen cloth and the business of Western-style clothing gangs are currently very prosperous.

Qiongzhou: 10th Shantou Hong Kong:

Continuous Demand for Gongxi Tea

The market already shows a supply shortage, a rare sight in recent years.

Gongxi silk tea has historically been primarily sold to Russia. In recent years, due to a sharp decline in sales from that source, tea merchants in various regions have changed their production methods, drastically reducing this year's Gongxi varieties to just over 30,000 boxes. Previously, due to active routes to India and continued procurement by Russian merchants, the market's existing stock was completely sold out. Recently, there have been multiple purchase requests from India, but supply cannot meet demand. This is an unprecedented situation in recent years. Zhenmei silk tea and local soil tea have also been mostly cleared out. Due to requests from abroad, firms such as Jinlong and Yihe are currently negotiating prices for one to two thousand boxes of incoming goods.

Sugar Market: New Quanzhou Sliced Qing Sugar Expected Soon

Yesterday, the sugar market trended flat. The guild’s prices were: No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar at 2.11.5 yuan per 50kg bag, transit sugar at 6.112 yuan. Dongbai sugar remained unchanged. However, No. 4 ( ) mark spot goods were 21.5 yuan. The factory’s refined white sugar was priced at 20.4 yuan. Guangdong and Chaozhou merchants offered over a hundred bags of "turned red" sugar at 14.215 to 14.115 yuan. Beihai sliced Qing sugar was also sold out at 10.4 yuan. The market outlook is tight, and it is reported that Quanzhou sliced Qing sugar will arrive soon.

Yesterday, the 合 company held its second tender for Guangdong sugar this week. The total quota was over 40,000 bags. They sold 590 bags of Shunde factory's Five Rams coarse white sugar at 21.3 yuan, and another 100 bags from the 市 factory at 21.1 yuan. The remaining sugar was not sold at the original price.

Miscellaneous: Despite Diplomatic Tensions, Japanese Imports Surge - How Should Japan Maintain Its Advantage?

In the past two months, despite Sino-Japanese diplomatic tensions and continued incitement of the Northeast border war, Japanese imports have surged more than before. The most significant categories include earthenware, lead sheets, lead blocks, bleaching powder, sulfuric acid, and salted fish. From Sunday to yesterday, there were three rounds of imports, totaling over 10,000 tons. It is reported that there are approximately 22,000 bags of sugar. Additionally, a Japanese ship that arrived yesterday carried over 1,000 packages of rayon, valued at over 300,000 yuan, in addition to sugar, lead sheets, and salted fish. Furthermore, in the past two months, Japanese imports have jumped to the top position. However, Japan remains unwilling to change its mindset and methods. If it were to drastically alter its plans, it could maintain its prosperity in trade with China for a long time. However, it does not pay attention to this, which is truly a pity.

Joint Announcement by Party and Government Agencies: Citizens Contribute One Day's Income, Set for December 12th, with Donations to Be Sent to Designated Banks

Guomin News reports that the city party headquarters and municipal government of this city have jointly issued an announcement to promote the One Day's Income Contribution to the Nation Campaign. They have designated December 12th as the day of contribution. The promotion committee also issued a notice to compatriots yesterday, stating that the nation and people are at a critical moment, and citizens should make the minimum sacrifice by contributing one day's income. The committee also sent letters to various agencies and organizations to take the lead. The resolution is recorded as follows:

Joint Announcement by Party and Government Agencies

The city party headquarters and municipal government of this city jointly issued an announcement yesterday to promote the One Day's Income Campaign, stating, "Regarding the joint announcement, the One Day's Income Contribution to the Nation Campaign Promotion Committee of this city submitted a report stating that the second item discussed at the second committee meeting was to designate December 12th as the day for the Shanghai citizens' One Day's Income Contribution Campaign, with attached measures for review. The resolution was passed. It was decided to request the party and government agencies to jointly issue an announcement, informing the general public to contribute one day's income, etc., as stated in the records. The original measures stipulated in the first item, requesting the party and government agencies to jointly issue an announcement to inform the general public to contribute one day's income, etc., are recorded. It is appropriate to record the case and submit it for review and action. The purpose of the One Day's Income Contribution Campaign in this city is to contribute the strength of the people to enrich national defense, which is a very good intention. The committee has now designated December 12th as the Shanghai citizens' One Day's Income Contribution Campaign day, which is feasible. It is appropriate to issue a joint announcement, urging all sectors of the city to comply. Except for those who have already contributed one day's income and have receipts from the receiving agencies, all citizens are urged to donate generously, and they must submit their salary income, business income, or profit income of that day to the designated Central, China, Communications, Shanghai, and Shanghai City Banks for collection, so as to gather strength and enrich our national defense. We have high hopes for this, and we hereby announce this."

Notice to Compatriots Issued by the Promotion Committee

The One Day's Income Contribution to the Nation Campaign Promotion Committee of this city issued a notice to compatriots yesterday, stating, "Dear compatriots, since the 'September 18th' Incident, our nation and people have been oppressed and invaded by others. Now, violent people are employing conspiracies and deceit to induce bandits and puppets to be their vanguard and invade our Suiyuan. For the sake of preserving the survival of the nation, the soldiers at the front are sacrificing their lives, fighting bloody battles with bandits and puppets in the icy and snowy lands. For a month, they have recovered Bailing Temple and Honggeertu, restoring our territory and establishing meritorious service beyond the Great Wall. Their blood has nurtured brilliant flowers and fruits, which deserves our infinite admiration and joy. However, when we think of our compatriots who are also Chinese, the soldiers at the front are charging into battle, bravely killing enemies, with severed limbs and remains lying on the battlefield. Can we, the compatriots in the rear, sit idly by? Now the weather is extremely cold. We feel cold even in our houses, so we can imagine how much harder it is for them to fight for the country in the fierce deserts of wind and snow. Since we cannot go to the front lines and share their hardships, we can only help them materially to show our respect and condolences. We firmly believe that all patriotic compatriots are thinking of those brave soldiers at the front who are killing enemies for the country and want to actively comfort them, giving them spiritual and material comfort to show that our spirit is connected with them. Therefore, in view of the patriotic enthusiasm of compatriots from all walks of life, we have launched the One Day's Income Campaign. The significance of the One Day's Income Campaign is to have all the people of the country rise up to assist the government in completing this great mission of suppressing bandits, resisting insults, and saving the country. Because the income of one person for one day is limited, but the concentrated one-day income of the people of the whole country is a very large number. Compatriots in the rear only sacrifice one day's income, while the soldiers at the front receive the condolences of compatriots in the rear, which can increase their courage to kill the enemy, and the effect will be great. Compatriots, the enemy is deep and the situation is urgent. The survival of the nation and people has reached a critical moment. One day's income is the minimum sacrifice that we citizens can make for the nation and people. Please rise up quickly and contribute your one day's income to the government to comfort the front lines, so as to show the great spirit of self-reliance of our Chinese nation. (Note) Please send the One Day's Income donation directly to the Central Bank, Bank of China, Communications Bank, Shanghai City Bank, and Shanghai Commercial Bank to receive a receipt. Manufactured by the One Day's Income Contribution to the Nation Campaign Promotion Committee of Shanghai City."

Agencies and Organizations Take the Lead

The promotion committee sent letters to various agencies and organizations, inviting them to take the lead in promoting the campaign among their employees and members. The letter stated, "Dear Sirs, The second item discussed at the second committee meeting of our committee was to designate December 12th as the day for the Shanghai citizens' One Day's Income Contribution Campaign, with attached measures for review. The resolution has been passed, and the meeting minutes have been printed and distributed. Regarding the progress, in addition to sending letters to party and government agencies, jointly issuing announcements to inform the general public to donate generously, and inviting various newspapers and radio stations to promote widely, and our committee issuing a notice to citizens to promote attention among all citizens, it seems that all agencies and organizations participating in our committee should take the lead in promoting the campaign, collecting the one-day income of their members and employees on that day, and submitting it to the bank designated by our committee to facilitate the process. In addition to sending separate letters, we hereby inform you, hoping that you will take note and handle it accordingly."

Designated Banks Collect Donations

The promotion committee previously resolved to invite the municipal government, the bankers' association, the accountants' association, the general labor union, the united university association, the citizen's association of the first special district, and the secondary school association to serve as donation management committee members, and designated the Central Bank, Bank of China, Communications Bank, Shanghai City Bank, and Shanghai Bank as donation collection agencies. It is now reported that the donation collection receipts have been sent to each of the banks. Agencies and organizations that have one-day campaign donations can send them to the Central Bank on the Bund, the Bank of China on Sanma Road, the Communications Bank on the Bund, the City Bank on Tianjin Road, and the Laosimen, Xinkaihe, and City Center branches of that bank, the Shanghai Bank on Ningbo Road, and the various branches and offices of that bank in this city for collection and withdrawal of receipts. It is also learned that the banks will immediately report to the association and publish the donations received in the newspapers.

Pang Jingzhou's Telegram: The Front Lines Urgently Need Supplies; North China Rescue Branch Established

When the Suiyuan war began, the general headquarters of the Chinese Red Cross Society in this city dispatched personnel to the front lines to inspect the condition of the wounded soldiers and implement rescue work. However, the local medicines and equipment were severely lacking. They telegraphed the headquarters to quickly prepare them and send a team to strengthen the effort. Personnel were dispatched to consult with various local groups on expanding the rescue work. It was generally agreed that the rescue work at the front lines was of great importance and that the name of the organization should be unified. It was deemed appropriate to strictly control the organization and ensure consistent use of the Red Cross flag and armband for identification to avoid disrupting military operations. The current policy of the association is: (1) to produce more wound dressings for use by wounded soldiers in battle; (2) to rush-produce medicine bags for rescuers to administer first aid; (3) to establish more wounded soldier hospitals; (4) to establish surgical teams composed of specialized surgeons carrying large surgical instruments and X-rays to perform surgeries in various wounded soldier hospitals. In order to increase work efficiency and facilitate local operations, a North China Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society Rescue Committee was established, inviting medical, pharmaceutical, commercial, and academic representatives from the Tianjin and Beijing areas to serve as committee members. It will be established soon. The association received a telegram from Pang Jingzhou from Suiyuan yesterday, stating that the local area is experiencing fierce north winds, snow-covered roads, and a need for warm clothing and bedding to be provided quickly. The vehicles and stretchers for transportation should also be rushed over. It is necessary to provide medicines such as cotton, gauze, bandages, yellow dye, carbolic acid, Lysol, hydrogen peroxide, knives, scissors, tweezers, injection solutions, and syringes. Because it is not easy to procure these in North China, the Shanghai headquarters must raise a large amount of materials. It is anticipated that a major war is imminent. Therefore, in addition to sending all stored items, the headquarters is actively soliciting the above materials, hoping that all sectors will quickly donate or assist in purchasing them with funds, so that they can be transported to the front lines as soon as possible to meet the urgent needs. Regardless of whether it is material or money, please send it to the Chinese Red Cross Society at 856 Xinzha Road. A receipt will be issued as proof. In addition to publishing thank-you notes and publishing a special record of credits, the general situation of rescue will be disclosed in the newspapers one by one.

Relief Conference Resolves to Transport First Batch of Winter Supplies

Since the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Local Self-Government Association, and Red Cross Society jointly formed the Suiyuan Bandit Suppression Relief and Rescue Committee and began collecting winter supplies, donations of silk wadded jackets, gloves, woolen shirts, etc., have been very enthusiastic. Yesterday, the executive committee resolved to transport the first batch, starting immediately. The details are as follows:

The executive committee held its third executive meeting at 4 p.m. the day before yesterday. Xiao Lai, Du Yuesheng, Liu Hongsheng, Shao Yanshan, Lin Kanghou, Mu Ouchu, Jin Runxiang, Huang Renzhi, Yan Esheng, and others attended. Xiao Lai chaired the meeting. First, the general secretary reported on the amount of donations and goods received, and then announced the following cases for discussion: (1) Transportation of Relief Goods Case. It was resolved that the first batch of winter supplies should be transported starting immediately, and Jin Runxiang was appointed to handle the matter. (2) Measures for Handling Relief Work Case. It was resolved that the rescue work should be actively handled by the Red Cross Society Rescue Committee in conjunction with the Rescue Work Promotion Association. The medicines received by the committee will be transferred to the Red Cross Society Rescue Committee at any time for immediate transport. As for the collected medicine packs, those that have already been received will also be transported first.

Telegrams from Fu Zuoyi: The City Chamber of Commerce and Local Self-Government Association previously received a telegram from Fu Zuoyi, which stated: "Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce and Local Self-Government Association, The recent Suiyuan alarm has attracted nationwide concern. I am grateful for your encouragement and spiritual support. The three armies are inspired and strengthened. We will strive to inspire ourselves and bravely kill the enemy, hoping to be loyal to the party and the country and live up to the earnest expectations of our patriotic compatriots. Special telegram to express our gratitude. Hope you will understand. Fu Zuoyi, with respect."

Joint Relief Association of Charitable Organizations Urges Donations of Money and Goods

Since its establishment, the Joint Relief Association of Charitable Organizations in Shanghai on Yunnan Road has spared no effort in appealing for action. It is particularly concerned about the refugees in the Suiyuan disaster area and is now actively urging donations of money and goods, and sending personnel to investigate the disaster situation. It previously telegraphed Director Yan Baichuan, requesting him to report the disaster situation in the war zone at any time. Yesterday, the association received a reply telegram from Director Yan, which is excerpted as follows: "To Mr. Kong Yongzhi, Chairman of the Shanghai Joint Relief Association of Charitable Organizations, and all colleagues, I have read your telegram. The bandits and puppets have invaded Suiyuan, and it is our duty to defend the territory. Thanks to the soldiers' efforts, we have achieved a small victory. I am ashamed to have received your praise. I am honored that your association is urging donations of money and goods and plans to send personnel to Suiyuan to relieve the people in the war zone and benefit the disaster victims. In the future, I will report the actual situation in the war zone at any time. Special telegram to express our gratitude, Yan Xishan, with respect."

Detained Rice Boats Released in Jiading; North Shanghai Resumes Business Yesterday Morning; Rice Prices Remain Stable Due to Active Sales from Various Groups; Representatives Who Petitioned in Jiangsu Province Have Returned to Shanghai

Representatives of various groups, including Gu Xin'yi, Jiang Zisheng, Lu Jingwen, Jiang Shizhi, and Lu Wenshao, from the City Chamber of Commerce, Local Self-Government Association, Bean and Rice Industry Association, Rice Shop Association, Rice Grain Merchants Association, and Changshu Guild Hall, traveled to Zhenjiang by car at 8 a.m. on the 8th to petition the provincial government. After arriving in the province, the representatives met with Chairman Chen, but due to Chairman Chen's illness, they were not received. The petition delegation then went to the Department of Civil Affairs to meet with Director Yu Jingtang. The secretary, Xiang Jutan, received them. The representatives submitted the official letters from various groups and reported in detail the incident of rice being detained in Jiading County, requesting immediate release to maintain the food supply for Shanghai citizens. The secretary agreed to immediately telegraph the county to release the detained rice boats. However, regarding the lifting of the rice ban, it would be discussed and handled by the Provincial Administrative Conference after receiving a clear order from the Executive Yuan. The representatives achieved satisfactory results and returned to Shanghai on the 6:20 p.m. express train that evening.

Detained Rice Released

After receiving the reply telegram from the Department of Civil Affairs of the Jiangsu Provincial Government on the afternoon of the 8th, the Jiading County Government immediately ordered the Second District Branch of the Nanxiang Public Security Bureau and the Jiading Temple Police Station to release the rice boats. All rice boats began to leave at 5 p.m. the night before last. The water level was low, and there were many boats, so they made every effort to dredge the waterway. The first batch of more than 80 rice boats arrived in Shanghai successively at 6-7 a.m. yesterday. The remaining large number of rice boats stranded in Huangdu and other places also arrived at the North Shanghai wharf successively in the afternoon.
