City Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed Request Not to Reduce Import Duties on Guangdong Foreign Rice

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance of the Executive Yuan yesterday, stating, "To the Ministry of Finance of the Executive Yuan in Nanjing, This year, all provinces have reported bumper harvests. Hunan, Anhui, and Jiangxi provinces are known as provinces that export surplus rice. It is appropriate to balance surpluses and deficits and support each other, so as to benefit the rural areas of Jiangsu and prevent losses. Guangdong Province has always relied on foreign rice for supplementation. During Chen Jitang's administration, he requested the central government to exempt Guangdong Province from import duties on foreign rice, which led to a large influx of foreign rice, resulting in a huge trade deficit in international trade. As a result, the rice markets in Wuhu and Guangdong Province have plummeted, and the national economy and people's livelihood have been affected. People with knowledge lament this. Fortunately, the tariff system has been unified, and Guangdong Province is levying import duties on foreign rice. In today's situation, when smuggling is rampant and customs revenues at Tianjin and Qinhuangdao have plummeted, it is not without benefit to the country and helps domestic rice compete with foreign rice, promoting sales in Guangdong Province, which is in line with the government's policy of regulating food and promoting rural prosperity. From the perspective of Guangdong, since the completion of the Yuehan Railway, it is convenient to transport Hunan rice to Guangdong, and the railway has also reduced freight rates to benefit both sides. Therefore, Guangdong Province is not in danger of lacking rice or eating expensive rice. Shantou also has Wuhu rice from Anhui Province, which is transferred from Jianglun to Shanghai and transported to Shantou, which is equally convenient. Moreover, according to rice merchants, the market price of domestic rice in Guangdong is only around 11 yuan, which is a clear indication that Guangdong rice has not become expensive. Guangdong Province has always taken the overall situation into consideration and will not indulge its habit of eating foreign rice and place the farmers of the whole country in a dilemma. It is a matter of urgency to maintain tariff integrity. Recently, it has been heard that the province has submitted a request to the central government to reduce or exempt import duties on foreign rice. Although it has not yet materialized, rice merchants in Guangdong and Anhui are very shocked, fearing that the agricultural products of the two provinces will have a surplus and repeat the so-called 'ripe famine' of the past. The matter is too important to remain silent. It is appropriate to telegram your esteemed Yuan (Ministry) for review and approval, and to preside over the matter, so that import duties on foreign rice in Guangdong Province will not be reduced or exempted, so as to maintain tariff integrity and save the countryside. We eagerly pray for this. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, respectfully."

As the End of the Gregorian Calendar Approaches, Both the Banking and Money Industries Are Handling Account Closures

Xinsheng News reports that the clearinghouses of the money industry close their accounts every year on the Lunar New Year's Eve. Now, the executive committee has decided that this year, the account closure will be handled once at the end of the Gregorian calendar. Members of the Money Industry Association have been notified to comply. The account closure period at the end of this year is approaching, and the money houses have complied with all procedures. Member banks of the Bankers Association handle account closures based on the Gregorian calendar. As the account closure period at the end of the year is approaching, all account closure procedures have been prepared. The association has also scheduled a meeting of member representatives at the end of this month to report on the association's affairs for the past six months and approve the budget and final accounts. This year, agricultural products in various parts of China have been harvested in abundance, resulting in stronger purchasing power among the people. All industries have reported active business, with the cotton textile industry being the most prosperous. Therefore, the account closures at the end of April, the end of October, the Dragon Boat Festival, and the Mid-Autumn Festival, when money houses have long-term credit loans, have all been passed smoothly. As for the account closure at the end of the Gregorian calendar, there is no other concern. It is expected that the account closure period for industry and commerce at the end of the Lunar calendar will also be passed smoothly.

Shengsi Islands Inspection Group Returns to Shanghai: Island Fisheries at Peak Producing 20 Million Yuan Annually, but Due to Encroachment by a Certain Country, Income is Only 3 Million Yuan

Since the Shengsi Islands were placed under the jurisdiction of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, various experts were specially invited to form the Shengsi Islands Inspection Group to develop the islands. On the 30th of last month, they departed from Wusong aboard the warship "Junhe." The group spent eight days on the Shengsi Islands and has now returned to Wusong on the same ship. Details are recorded below.

Participants included Zheng Yitong, Committee Member and Jiangsu Provincial Committee Member; Ge Tan, Administrative Inspector of the Fourth District of Jiangsu; Hou Zhaohai, Chief of the First Section of the Fisheries and Animal Husbandry Department of the Ministry of Industry; Tang Chengzong, Managing Director of the Shanghai Fish Market, and representative Liang Teng; Zhu Aizhou, District Chief of the Third District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police; Qu Junyuan, representative of the Fisheries Syndicate of the Ministry of Industry and Director of the Shanghai Social Bureau Fisheries Guidance Center; Gu Hongxi, Magistrate of Chongming County; Tang Huisun, Head of the Agricultural Science Department of Nantong College; Hong Shige, Head of the Medical Science Department; Yang Guanbei, Manager of Dada Steamship Company; Yao Yongchang, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Fisheries Experiment Station; Wang Wentai, Technician of the Jiangsu Construction Department, and over twenty others, including Lu Yanghao and Zhang Pijie.

Group Divisions: The group boarded the "Junhe" warship at 3:00 PM on the 30th of last month and headed south. That evening at 7:00 PM, they anchored in the waters of Tongsha overnight. The group leaders, Ge Tan and Zheng Yitong, convened a meeting, and the result was the division into seven inspection groups: (1) Civil Affairs Group, divided into: 1. Baojia (local administration system); 2. Militia training; 3. Prohibition of opium, gambling, and prostitution; 4. Fishermen's organizations; 5. Local customs and sentiments; 6. Food supply; 7. Afforestation and scenery. Members of this group: Zheng Yitong, Ge Tan, Gu Hongxi. (2) Transportation Group, divided into: 1. Ships; 2. Docks; 3. Roads; 4. Postal and telecommunications; 5. Transportation; 6. Fishing ports. Members of this group: Yang Guanbei, Tang Chengzong. (3) Economic Group, divided into: 1. Land; 2. Taxes; 3. Cooperation; 4. Finance; 5. Sideline occupations; 6. Yellow sand; 7. Social economy; 8. Fishery trading relationships. Members of this group: Hou Zhaohai, Tang Huisun, Qu Junyuan, Liang Teng, Lu Yanghao, Zhang Pijie. (4) Public Security Group, divided into: 1. Police; 2. Defense Corps; 3. Firearms; 4. Officers and soldiers; 5. Expenses; 6. Water Police. Members of this group: Zhu Aizhou, Ge Tan, Gu Hongxi, Zhang Anyuan. (5) Education Group, divided into: 1. Private schools; 2. Elementary schools; 3. Fishermen's continuing education; 4. Liaison between aquatic schools and the island; 5. Fishermen's level of knowledge. Members of this group: Qu Junyuan, Gu Hongxi, Hou Zhaohai. (6) Fisheries Group, divided into: 1. Types of fish products and nearby fishing grounds; 2. Types of fisheries; 3. Mariculture; 4. Sale and transportation of aquatic products; 5. Fishing and salt; 6. Construction related to fisheries; 7. Fishermen's economy. Members of this group: Wang Wentai, Tang Chengzong, Hou Zhaohai, Qu Junyuan, Yao Yongnian, Liang Teng, Yang Yue'an, Cao Erwei, Shao Piaoliu. (7) Health Group, divided into: 1. Fish parasites and their relationship to humans; 2. Fishermen's occupational diseases; 3. Health administration and treatment; 4. Fishing ground inspection stations. Members of this group: Zhou Liang, Hong Shilü.

Inspection Process: The group arrived at Sijiao on the morning of the 1st of this month and immediately inspected the local land and sea military police. They then divided into groups for inspection. On the 2nd, they remained in Sijiao to continue inspecting Xiaoyangshan and Huadaoshan. On the 4th and 5th, they inspected Shengshan, Donglvhua Mountain, and Xilvhua Mountain. On the 6th, they inspected Gouqi Mountain. On the morning of the 7th, they inspected Shengshan again. After the inspection, they took the original ship back to Shanghai.

Overview of the Islands: The Shengsi

Islands comprise more than ten large and small islands in the ocean off the borders of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, north of the Zhoushan Archipelago and Chongming Island. Due to jurisdictional issues, Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces had long disputed their governance. At the end of October, the Executive Yuan finally approved that they would remain under the jurisdiction of Jiangsu Province. The fisheries of these islands are extremely prosperous, accounting for over 90% of the islands' total economy, and are the best in the southeastern provinces, with an annual output of nearly 20 million yuan. However, due to frequent incursions by fishing boats from a certain country, the income of the island fishermen is only 3 million yuan. The island's facilities are also very rudimentary, and construction of transportation, water, electricity, and other infrastructure is lacking. After this group's inspection, each group has drafted reports and proposed improvement suggestions, which have been submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for forwarding to the central government for review and approval. It is said that the island's geographical situation is also of great importance to national defense.

Steamship Industry Association Submits to the Ministry: Flexible Restrictions on Purchasing Old Ships, Our Country's Industry is Immature, Not Suitable to Cut the Feet to Fit the Shoes, Contributes Two Points of Flexible Measures Based on Facts

The Shanghai Steamship Industry Association has requested the Ministry of Transportation to waive the age limit on ship purchases and has contributed flexible opinions. The original text is as follows: Submitted to address the hindrance to the development of the shipping industry due to restrictions on the age of ship purchases. We respectfully submit a written opinion containing the facts of difficulties collected from shipping merchants and requests for flexible measures. We respectfully request your kind review and approval for implementation. We received a letter from the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, stating that the Ministry had instructed that in recent years, shipping merchants have often purchased old and dilapidated foreign ships. If not strictly restricted, it would affect navigation safety. In the future, the purchase of old ships should be reported for review, and the age of cargo ships should not exceed twenty years, and the age of passenger ships should not exceed fifteen years. The letter instructed to inform all industry members to comply. Considering the opinions of shipping merchants, the restriction on ship age is indeed inappropriate. We detailed the reasons and requested the Maritime Affairs Bureau to forward it to the Ministry, requesting a delay in implementation. We received a reply that the Ministry instructed that it should not be discussed. While transmitting this, we also received a letter from the Navigation Affairs Department of the Ministry, stating that the three draft plans for consolidating the shipping industry had already accommodated the shipping merchants' requests and had been reviewed and approved. However, Article 17 of the Supervision Regulations, which restricts ship age, will not be changed because it already has a ministerial order. Shipping merchants were disappointed upon hearing this. As this matter is of great importance to the future of the shipping industry, after a joint discussion by all industry members, they believe that restricting the age of ship purchases is not only a personal issue for shipping merchants but also greatly affects the rise and fall of the national shipping industry and the gains and losses of the national economy. Various facts have been collected from each member to prove that the restriction is not timely. Now, we respectfully submit a written opinion containing the facts of difficulties and requests for flexible measures, requesting your kind review and approval for implementation. We are extremely apprehensive and await orders. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Transportation.

Attached are the opinions on the facts of difficulties in restricting the age of ship purchases and requests for flexible measures. Opinions on restricting the age of ship purchases: (1) Our country's shipping industry is still in its infancy. Statistics show that the total tonnage of all commercial ships in the country (above 500 tons) is only 447,000 tons, which is less than 1% compared to the total number of ships worldwide (above 500 tons). The United Kingdom and the United States have developed maritime transport and are the leaders in the world, with ship tonnage exceeding 10 million tons. We are far behind them, but countries such as Japan, Germany, Italy, France, and the Netherlands are in the range of 2 to 4 million tons. Even small countries such as Greece and Denmark have more than 1 million tons of commercial ships. With the vast territory, large population, and long coastline of our country, we only have this small amount of tonnage. Upon examination, it is indeed dwarfed in comparison. We should plan to expand and increase tonnage to enhance our international position. Now, by restricting the age of ship purchases, it is like cocooning ourselves, and from then on, our country's shipping industry will inevitably decline, which is contrary to the main purpose of promoting development. (2) Our country has few shipyards, and what they can build is only light-tonnage ships. Although the government has promulgated shipbuilding incentive regulations, even if the order is implemented, the bonuses obtained according to the current shipbuilding prices are less than one-tenth. Therefore, although shipbuilding is encouraged, it is still difficult to achieve practical results. The construction of new ships is unlikely to happen. If the age of ship purchases is restricted abruptly, it will inevitably lead to fewer old ships and no new ships being built, and the shipping industry will be even more diminished. (3) Our country is bound by treaties and cannot prevent foreign merchant ships from sailing. Currently, foreign merchants operating in our country's coastal and Yangtze River shipping (ships above 500 tons): British firm Butterfield & Swire has 65 ships, totaling 162,000 tons; Jardine Matheson has 34 ships, totaling 95,000 tons; Japanese firm Nissin Kisen has 26 ships, totaling 56,000 tons, totaling 313,000 tons. The tonnage of these three companies alone accounts for three-quarters of the number of ships in our country. If we add the British firm Laiji and the Japanese firms Dalian and Osaka, their tonnage will exceed the number of ships in our entire country. Their strength and intense competition are far beyond what our country can match. If we further restrict the purchase of ships by Chinese people, it will only allow foreign merchants to take advantage of the opportunity to develop and increase their power. (4) In the past, when Japan's shipping industry was not developed, shipping merchants competed to purchase old ships from other countries to expand their shipping business, and the government did not restrict them. Recently, the country began to gradually restrict the purchase of old ships because the shipbuilding industry has developed, but Japanese shipping merchants still have more than 40 old ships operating under the flags of other countries to obscure their business. The drawbacks of restrictions can be imagined. Moreover, countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, France, and Norway have old ships accounting for more than one-third or even half of the total number of ships, but there is no order prohibiting the purchase of old ships. Our country's shipping industry is lagging behind, and the situation is even more different. If we do not investigate the actual situation and hastily imitate Japan to restrict old ships, it is equivalent to cutting the feet to fit the shoes, which is not appropriate. (5) The safety of ship navigation should pay attention to the quality of the ship, but more importantly, the prudence of driving, the appropriateness of management, the strictness of inspection, the completeness of equipment, and the perfection of repairs are the most important keys. New ships sailing, even if encountering hurricanes, thick fog, or the other party's ships accidentally steering into the waterway, or due to tidal currents and not knowing the collision avoidance regulations, are not absolutely exempt from the occurrence of danger. As for those who drive old ships, if they can be cautious every step of the way, be familiar with navigation technology, and be able to handle emergencies, it may not necessarily lead to accidents. Moreover, when shipping merchants purchase ships now, they must first examine the ship's detailed list of internal contents and must also pass the examination of Lloyd's or other reliable ship experts to check the iron plates under the waterline and boilers and other procedures. After sailing into the country, when registering with the Maritime Affairs Bureau, technical personnel must measure and conduct special inspections before being allowed to sail. Therefore, the safety issue of old ships is no different from that of new ships. The above points are all based on facts. Once examined, it can be clearly seen that restricting the age of ship purchases is not suitable for today's shipping merchants. It is very clear. Now that the Ministry's order has not been withdrawn and the regulations have not been revised, shipping merchants feel deeply and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we dare to list the facts and make another petition, requesting your consideration and appropriate flexibility to avoid obstruction. There are two flexible measures: (1) Divide the size of the tonnage and make the scope of restrictions. First, implement restrictions on ships below 200 tons, and temporarily waive the implementation for ships above 200 tons. (2) Determine the restriction period according to the increase in tonnage. Currently, the total number of commercial ships in the country is less than 500,000 tons. When it increases to one million tons, implement the restriction. When it increases to more than 750,000 tons but less than one million tons, the age limit should be increased by ten years according to the current ministerial order. This flexible handling can be consistent with the Ministry's order, and the difficulties of the shipping industry can also be taken care of.

Yang Wendao and Ye Haisheng's Appeals Were Rejected. Yang et al. Expressed Dissatisfaction in Court and Will Appeal to the Supreme Court.

Yang Wendao and Ye Haisheng, both from Guangdong, were accused of assassinating Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo in Hongkou last winter. After the police investigation identified them as the perpetrators, they were prosecuted. The First Special District Court initially sentenced them to death. Yang and Ye were dissatisfied and, through their defense lawyers, filed an appeal with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Presiding Judge Yu convened a collegiate panel on the 2nd of this month, ordering Yang and Ye to present their case. After a full day of investigation and deliberation, the debate was declared closed, and the public pronouncement was scheduled for the afternoon of the 9th. Yang and Ye were returned to the Western Prison by the police. Yesterday at 2 PM, the time for the verdict arrived. Presiding Judge Yu, along with Judges Zhou and Nie, Prosecutor Lin, and court clerks, ascended the bench in the First Criminal Court. Lawyer Ru Baoyi, representing the police, and the defense lawyers for Yang and Ye, all arrived in court. Then, the detectives brought Yang and Ye from the holding cell to stand before the court. Presiding Judge Yu stood and read the verdict, the main text of which stated, "The appeal is rejected." He further instructed that if they were dissatisfied with this verdict, they could appeal to the Supreme Court within ten days of receiving the written verdict. Yang and Ye both expressed their dissatisfaction and stated they would file an appeal.

The City Was as Dark as Night: Heavy Fog Yesterday Morning Affected Air and Sea Traffic; Shops Had to Operate with Lights On

After the atmosphere in this city turned cold, there have already been two instances of fog. Although it drifted and dissipated intermittently, the weather has turned cold. Yesterday morning, heavy fog returned, thick and condensed, making it impossible to see even at close range. Traffic was greatly affected. The Associated Press reporter has recorded the following details:

Dense Fog

The day before yesterday afternoon, there was a brief period of sleet. The weather was gloomy all day. Yesterday at dawn, heavy fog suddenly arose, thick and impenetrable. It was difficult to distinguish people and objects even at close range. All kinds of vehicles on the streets drove with their lights on, and businesses had to operate with their electric lights on. The city was dark, resembling a night scene. After 9 AM, heavy rain resumed, making the fog even denser.

Waterway Closure

Imports and exports, ships, were all suspended until 11:00 AM this morning due to the heavy fog. Ships held up outside the Wusongkou included the Xin Beijing on the Shanghai-Ningbo route, the Long'an on the Shanghai-Guangdong route, the Wuxue on the Yangtze River route, and the Shengjing on the Northern Seas route. Vessels held up in the Huangpu River included about five or six ships such as the Huangpu on the Yangtze River route and the Haiheng on the Shanghai-Guangdong route.

Delayed Flights

At the same time, the waters of the Huangpu River were mixed with fog, creating a very dense atmosphere. Apart from the Bopu ferry, which was still slowly moving with its lights on, all other boats were suspended. The Shanghai-Hankou-Westbound flights of the China National Aviation Corporation, as well as the Shanghai-Ping-Northbound flights, were also delayed. Traffic only resumed gradually after the fog dissipated in the afternoon.

Construction of Guide Dikes at the Mouth of the Huangpu River

A reporter from Zhongzhou News Agency learned from the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau yesterday that the guide dikes built by the bureau at the mouth of the Huangpu River have now been fully completed. Construction of this guide dike began in 1907 on the left bank of the river, with the dike shaped in a semi-circle. The purpose of this dike is to limit the cross-current of the tide to one side. At the same time, the depth of the water in the Huangpu River can be increased from seventeen feet to twenty-five feet. The entire project cost 1 million yuan. Ocean-going vessels with heavier tonnage can also smoothly enter the port without having to anchor outside the Wusongkou. Eight years later, Chederan, the chief engineer of the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau, proposed building a similar guide dike on the side of the Huangpu River. However, this dike is simpler than the previous one, and the materials used are mainly willow wood and small stones, with a length of one English mile. Now that this dike has been completed, the depth of the Huangpu River can be increased by several more feet. Ships can come and go without being affected by high or low tides. In the future, the bureau plans to extend the dike towards the Longhua River surface.

A Tourist Angrily Took Poison After Being Slapped by a Dancer

Shi Lianbao, a 25-year-old from Fenghua, residing at No. 63 Yongji Lane, Datong Road, went to the Juelu Dance Hall on Yu Qiaqing Road to dance the night before last. He had a quarrel with dancer Chen Lili and was slapped in the face by the dancer. Shi left quickly. At 6:30 last night, Shi swallowed sleeping pills and staggered back to the Juelu Dance Hall to reason with Chen. Unexpectedly, the poison took effect suddenly, and he collapsed. The dance hall staff, realizing he had taken poison, reported to the police and sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment by ambulance.

Lawyer Ji ZongSui Is Accused of Public Insult Due to Defending a Litigant. Lawyer Ji Denies Any Intention to Insult.

Lawyer Ji ZongSui joined the Shanghai Lawyers Association as a member in August of the 19th year of the Republic [1930], and set up his office on the 5th floor of the Continental Commercial Building on Nanjing Road. Recently, Sun Jisheng, the owner of Ruichang Clothing Store at 1243 Huade Road, filed a criminal suit against Lawyer Ji with the First Special Court, accusing him of violating Article 309 of the Criminal Code for publicly insulting him. The main points of the indictment were as follows: The plaintiff and the defendant, Ji ZongSui, did not know each other. At 11:00 AM on the 26th of last month,

First Special Court

Criminal Court One Judge Feng Shide was hearing the case of Zhang Linqing and Zhang Sun vs. Hou Guangren et al. for assault. When Hou Guangren's defense lawyer, Ji ZongSui, made his statement, he publicly declared that "Hou Guangren has a daughter, Hou Xiuqin, who broke away from the Weng family and received 8,000 yuan for living expenses, and was then seduced by Sun Jisheng, Zhang Linqing's nephew, who coveted Hou's wealth and beauty," etc. Miu Baosheng and others who were in the audience at the time heard this. This clearly constitutes

The crime of public insult." Upon receiving the complaint, the court, led by Judge Dai, convened a hearing in Criminal Court Two yesterday afternoon. The plaintiff, Sun Jisheng, recounted the previous events, stating that the defendant's insulting remarks in court were heard by my legal counsel, Lawyer Shi Jiutang, who then relayed them to me, hence the lawsuit. When questioned, the defendant Ji ZongSui argued that I appeared in court in another case as a defender, and during the debate, I mentioned Sun Jusheng. However, the suit was brought against Sun Jisheng. Not only are the characters "Ju" and "Ji"

Different in meaning, their pronunciations are also different. The plaintiff in the lawsuit, therefore, is inaccurate. Furthermore, I was at the time clarifying and explaining matters directly related to the dispute based on the statements of both parties, doing my best to defend and attack, which is an obligation that a defense lawyer should fulfill. There is absolutely no question of criminal intent. If a defense lawyer is convicted for this, then in the future, defense lawyers, when appearing in court, can only

Pretend to be mutes. Moreover, I do not know the plaintiff and had no intention of insulting him. Since the plaintiff was not present when the other case was heard, it is impossible for my remarks to cause him discomfort based on Lawyer Shi's recounting, and thus it does not meet the requirements for insult. In terms of substance, not only did the defendant in the other case confess that Hou Xiuqin was

Seduced and eloped with Jisheng, but also the plaintiff's agent, Lawyer Shi, admitted in court in the other case that Hou Xiu had an affair with Zhang Linqing's store partner. These points can all be verified by the trial transcript. I request that I be declared innocent." The court announced the debate closed and set the verdict for the 14th of this month.

Mr. Jiang Zuling, Manager of Hua Hua Pen Factory, Steals Gold Pen Nibs to Exchange for Money, Totaling 290 Dozen Worth Over 3,000 Yuan, Takes Them to a Silver Shop to Melt Down, Obtaining Over 1,000 Yuan in Gold, Jiang, Burdened with Debt After Marriage, Conceived a Wild Idea

Jiang Zuling, a native of Ningbo, residing at No. 57 Dexing Lane, Disicheng Road, was appointed as the manager of the Hua Hua Fountain Pen Factory at No. 39 Bowuyuan Road in the spring of this year. The factory was established by Xu Deren, a Ningbo merchant dealing in tobacco, who was a close friend of Jiang. Therefore, when Jiang was appointed as the manager, he also invested 300 yuan of capital. Jiang has been in charge for seven months, and the factory's business has been quite prosperous. However, Jiang is over thirty years old and has not yet married. Through matchmaking, he married a Miss Ge on the 16th of last month. However, Jiang had no permanent assets, and the marriage resulted in heavy debts. Recently, due to creditors' demands for repayment, Jiang was unable to pay. Out of desperation, on the afternoon of the 2nd of this month at 1:00 PM, he took 290 dozen fountain pen nibs (each nib containing 60% gold content), valued at 3,200 yuan, from the factory to the Lao Tianbao Silver Shop on Nanyang Bridge in the French Concession and exchanged them for 1,202 yuan and 7 jiao and 1 fen in national currency. After obtaining the money, Jiang did not go to the factory to work. After Xu learned of this, he reported it to the General Inspectorate. Detectives Song Yuanshan and Bao Tan Ni Jiaxin were instructed to investigate. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, they finally found Jiang, his wife Jiang Ge, and his mother-in-law Ge Lin hiding in Room 106 of the Tongshang Hotel on Avenue Edward VII. They rushed to arrest them and brought them back to the police station. They found 30 silver dollars on Jiang, 55 yuan on Jiang Ge, and 1,000 yuan in Ge Lin's pocket. An investigation at Lao Tianbao revealed that the gold had already been melted down. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Ru Baoyi prosecuted them under Articles 30 and 336 of the Criminal Law. Subsequently, Jiang Deren reported that there were still fountain pens and accounts, and it was not yet clear whether there was any further embezzlement. When questioned, Jiang Zuling confessed that he committed the crime due to marriage debts. He claimed that his mother-in-law was unaware of the matter and wept incessantly. After Judge Qian Hongye of the Criminal Division questioned Jiang Ge and Ge Lin, he ordered the case to be adjourned for further questioning. Jiang Ge and Ge Lin were released and ordered to appear in court for the next hearing.

Fuyuan Theater: A Visitor Fires a Gun While Meeting a Friend, Wu Linlin Arrested and Taken to the Police Station

Xu Shunqing, a 50-year-old native of Pudong, established the Fuyuan Theater on Avenue Joffre in Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon at 2:50 PM, while a play was being performed, Wu Linlin, a 46-year-old native of Nantong, residing at No. 10 Puan Lane, Minquan Road, French Concession, went to the theater to look for actor Wang Guoxiang. Zhang Hualin, a 29-year-old Shandong native who was collecting tickets at the theater, stopped him from entering, and the two got into an argument. The argument escalated into a fight. Wu Linlin took out a pistol from his pocket and fired two shots. At the time, there were over two hundred theatergoers inside the theater. Upon hearing the shots, they suspected it was a robbery and fled in different directions, causing chaos. Wu ran out of the theater after firing the shots. Police officers arrived and apprehended Wu Linlin, confiscating a Browning pistol containing six bullets. He was taken to the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau for questioning and will be transferred to the General Bureau for handling.

Chief of Gaoqiao Public Security Bureau Accused of Embezzling Bonuses, Trial Concluded Yesterday, Sentence to be Announced on a Scheduled Date

Wang Songfu, Xing Sigui, and others, former police officers at the Gaoqiao Branch of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau in Pudong, filed a private lawsuit in the local court against Guo Bin, an eighteen-year-old patrol officer, and Tang Jinghuan, a forty-five-year-old chief of the branch bureau, accusing them of embezzling 270 yuan, 0 jiao, 1 fen, and 6 li of bonus money. The case was heard by Judge Xie Zhengong yesterday. The plaintiffs stated that on March 27, they discovered smuggled rayon on the Yuxing steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. They were awarded 436 yuan and 9 jiao and 6 fen by their superiors, but Tang and Guo embezzled it. They claimed that they had only received 166 yuan and 8 jiao approved by the General Bureau and requested the recovery of 270 yuan, 0 jiao, 1 fen, and 6 li. They also claimed that on September 4, he gave me fifty yuan, but I do not know for what reason. I didn't hand it in to the treasury and transferred me to the General Bureau etc. The judge stated that regarding the private lawsuit, according to customs regulations, it should be transferred to the civil court and cannot be attached to the criminal lawsuit. The plaintiffs agreed to transfer the civil lawsuit to the civil court. The judge then questioned Tang Jinghuan, who stated that after discovering the smuggled goods in March, according to the usual bonus distribution, the branch chief should receive 50%, the superior officer should receive 25%, and the officers who solved the case should receive 25%. However, since it was the initial resolution of the case, the General Bureau was reported and they got 40% each, they all got it. Later, because they had a fight, they were transferred to the General Bureau and have now been fired, so they hold a grudge and falsely accuse me and requested dismissal and filed a counterclaim. Guo Bin also stated that he led the search for the smuggled goods. His statement was similar to Tang's. The judge concluded the debate and scheduled the sentence to be announced at 10:00 AM on the 14th of this month.

Tianfaxiang Fur Store: Female Swindler Apprehended, Grey Overcoat Not Lost, Female Swindler Thrown in Jail

At around 11:00 AM, as the Tianfaxiang Fur Store at No. 390 Henan Road was preparing to close, a modernly dressed female customer arrived. The store clerks greeted her and asked what she wanted to buy. She identified herself as Deng Chengli, a 27-year-old native of Henan, and said she wanted a grey overcoat. She selected one priced at 88 yuan, put it on, and asked the store clerks to accompany her home to get the money. She hired a Xiang Sheng taxi, and Tianfaxiang sent store clerks Zhu Chunmao and Hong Futang to go with her. The taxi drove to the intersection of North Henan Road and Laobazi Road and stopped. They entered the Yanqing Lane and went to No. 7 Kangheng Printing House. Deng asked the two clerks to wait outside while she went inside to get the money from her husband. However, Zhu and Hong, knowing that there were many scams recently, suspected foul play and refused her request. Deng had no choice but to return to the store with the two clerks. Suspecting that Deng's actions were suspicious, they called the police (No. 468) and had Deng Chengli arrested and taken to the General Inspectorate. Under questioning, she firmly denied any intention to swindle and refused to reveal her address. After two hours of questioning, she finally admitted that she lived at No. 54 Yongan Lane, North Sichuan Road. Police officers were sent to search her residence and found nine pawn tickets. Deng was transferred to the women's prison for detention. Yesterday morning, she was escorted to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu prosecuted her for attempted fraud under Article 339, Section 3 of the Criminal Law, and stated that the police found nine pawn tickets in the defendant's residence, suggesting other possible offenses. It was also discovered that the defendant had previously been fined ten yuan for soliciting male customers. He requested an adjournment. The defendant Deng Chengli denied the charges, claiming that she was being framed by the Tianfaxiang Fur Store. Judge Pan ordered the defendant to be detained and remanded for further questioning in seven days.

Robbery Case on Zhoujiazui Road: Deceased Thief Identified, Autopsy Approved

On the afternoon of the day before yesterday at 7:00 PM, the Xietai Grain Store at No. 157 Zhoujiazui Road was broken into by four robbers who brandished guns and demanded silence. They stole 70 yuan in legal tender and silver coins before fleeing. The owner, Gu Shuitao, a native of Pudong, reported the incident to the Jiaxing Road Police Station by telephone. Detectives Cao Jinbiao and Liu Zhongcheng, along with nearby patrol officers, were dispatched to apprehend the robbers. The robbers resisted arrest. As a result, one of the robbers, Wang Xiaosan from Nanjing, was captured, and another robber was shot and wounded and sent to the police hospital for treatment. He died from his injuries. The body was sent to the Ferry Road Morgue. Wang was taken to the police station for detention. Details of the case have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. A passerby, Zhou Keming, was injured and is being treated at Tongren Hospital. The defendant stated in his police confession that he had recently arrived in Shanghai from his hometown and stayed with friends Luo Fuyuan and Zhu Lanting at No. 18 Yucai Lane in Zhabei. Unable to find work, Luo and Zhu invited him to rob Xietai. He stood guard outside. The police sent Chinese and foreign detectives to Zhabei, together with detectives from the Public Security Bureau, to arrest the accomplices who had fled elsewhere. They only found a bundle of stolen banknotes totaling 18 yuan and 6 jiao. Because the banknotes were tied with rubber bands, they could be identified and asked for an extension. Gu Shuitao, the owner, and apprentices Xi Maogou and Li Jinshun from the store, testified to the events. The detectives found two fake ironwood pistols at the scene and kept them for inspection. When questioned, Wang’s testimony was evasive. Judge Xiao Xiefen ordered him to be detained for further investigation. The body of the deceased Liu was inspected by prosecutor Song from the court, who determined that the unidentified robber had died from gunshot wounds sustained before death. An autopsy was approved by the forensic research institute, and the body was handed over to Ah Shan Villa for burial.

The Shanghai Municipal Council Scheduled Inspection of Carts

Public Concession "Type B" carts are hand-drawn carts that carry 500 pounds or less. According to regulations, they must be inspected once a year. The inspection period for this year has been set from December 14th to the 31st. During this period, all cart owners should send their carts to the Fairness Road rickshaw inspection office for inspection.

Dancer Zhu Menglan Accuses of Attempted Rape and Assault, Defendant is Du Baosheng, Owner of Royal Dance Hall, Court Questioned Plaintiff Yesterday

Zhu Menglan, a Guangdong woman also known as Zhu Meilan, 21 years old, residing at No. 170 Meidexing Lane, No. 176 Peng Road, who worked as a dancer at the Yangtze Dance Hall and other places, recently filed a criminal complaint with the First Special District Court through lawyer Yan Enliang, accusing Du Baosheng, the owner of the Royal Dance Hall at No. 65 Chang'an Lane, Wusong Road, and his wife, of attempted rape and assault, causing injuries. She requested that they be punished according to Article 277 of the Criminal Law. Because Zhu only wrote "Boss Du" in the complaint when she went to the court for an injury examination, the court summoned Zhu Menglan to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special Court yesterday afternoon for investigation to clarify the matter. Questioned by Judge Dai Rongduo, Zhu Menglan stated that because of poverty, she learned to dance. In November of this year, she was introduced to the Royal Dance Hall on Zhubaoshan Road to work as a dancer. The owner, Du Baosheng, coveted her beauty and forced her to engage in improper behavior. Because she refused, he held a grudge. On the morning of the 26th of last month at 11:00 AM, he incited another dancer to lure her to the defendant's residence and falsely accused her of defaming his reputation. He and his wife severely beat her, causing injuries to her abdomen and legs. She reported the incident to the Hongkou Police Station. She was treated by Dr. Gong Yan and went to the court for an injury examination. Lawyer Yan Enliang stated that it has been determined that the defendant "Boss Du's" real name is Baosheng, so another complaint has been filed with the court to request that the case be heard and investigated. After verifying the testimony, Judge Dai ordered the case to be adjourned to the afternoon of the 16th to summon the defendants Du Baosheng and his wife for further questioning.

Andersson to Give a Lecture Today: Ancient Hun Bronze Artifacts

Dr. Andersson, Director of the Museum of Far Eastern Antiquities in Stockholm, Sweden, is scheduled to give a public lecture at the Asian Cultural Society, No. 20 Bowuyuan Road, at 5:30 PM today. The topic is "Ancient Hun Bronze Artifacts." Dr. Andersson is a renowned expert in geology and archeology. He served as a geological advisor to the Chinese government for more than ten years and made many contributions to geological research in China. He also explored the Arctic and Antarctic regions and wrote many books. The discovery of the "Peking Man" bones in Zhoukoudian was due to Dr. Andersson's initial discovery of a human tooth fossil there. Later, he discovered China's first stone village in Henan Province and cultural artifacts from the Stone Age, Bronze Age, and Iron Age in Gansu Province. He discovered new departments of Stone Age colored pottery. Dr. Andersson is an expert on ancient Hun bronze artifacts. Anyone interested in antiques should attend his lecture.

Warning: Beware of Being Deceived When Purchasing Fire Extinguishers

According to the Shanghai Municipal Council, there are now unscrupulous merchants in the concession who wear uniforms similar to those worn by personnel of the Public Concession Fire Department. They break into small factories run by Chinese and inspect under false pretenses. They sell fire extinguishers and use alarming language, as if they were acting under orders and purchase is unavoidable. Merchants lacking knowledge are often deceived and buy cheap fire extinguishers and other equipment at exorbitant prices. The police of the Municipal Council are paying close attention to this matter. If merchants encounter such incidents, they can inquire at the Fire Department, which will provide guidance. Merchants can avoid wasting money. The Fire Department does not sell fire extinguishers.

Gong Xikui Sued for Alimony by Divorced Wife, Owed Over 1,000 Yuan in Alimony, Gong Has Left Shanghai and Cannot Be Served

Gong Xikui, former magistrate of Suining County, inspector-general of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, and chief of the Xinzha branch of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, married Li Manying (now 27 years old, residing at No. 112 Qingtai Road, Hangzhou), a woman from Hang County, in Hangzhou seven years ago. They married and lived together in Hangzhou, but did not have any children. Recently, Gong has taken a new lover and built a golden house at No. 7 Chongde Lane, Luban Road, French Concession, ignoring Li. This caused a breakdown in their relationship. The two divorced by agreement in Shanghai on January 15 of this year. An agreement was signed, certified by a lawyer, stipulating that Gong would pay Li 5,000 yuan in alimony in installments. The agreement stated that 500 yuan would be paid within one week of the signing date, 200 yuan would be paid at the end of February, 300 yuan would be paid in March and April, and 120 yuan would be paid every month starting at the end of May until the full amount of 5,000 yuan was paid. However, after signing the divorce agreement, Gong only paid the first installment of 500 yuan. No further payments have been made, and as of the end of November, he owes 1,520 yuan, which he has ignored. Unable to make a living, Li hired a lawyer to send a letter urging Gong to pay, but to no effect. Li Manying has hired lawyer Yuan Yang'an to file a lawsuit in the Civil Division of the Second Special Court against Gong, requesting that the court order the defendant to pay the overdue amount of 1,520 yuan. The court accepted the complaint and, in early December, Judge Wu Xiaoke convened a hearing in the Civil Division. The process server tried to serve Gong Xikui, the defendant, at his residence but was unable to do so as he was not in Shanghai, and nobody accepted the summons. Only the plaintiff, represented by lawyer Yuan, stated the facts of the lawsuit and requested a judgment on the subject matter, interest, and legal costs to be borne by the defendant, that the defendant's whereabouts are unknown and impossible to subpoena, and requested a public notice. The court reviewed the circumstances and adjourned the hearing to subpoena the defendant for further examination.

Yang Emerald Store on Liangting Road, City, Child Burned to Death, Fire Breaks Ladder, Child Thrown from Window Upstairs, Pregnant Housewife and Partner Jump Out of Window Injured, Spreads to Neighbors, Bird Store and Small World

At 7:45 yesterday morning, a fire broke out on the upper floor of the Wang Baofeng Yang Emerald Store at No. 16 Liangting Road, west of Fuyou Road, Xinbeimen, Nanshi, due to cooking breakfast and using a gas stove. Although the fire departments of the nearby Chenghuangmiao and Nanshi districts dispatched vehicles to rescue the situation, the streets there were narrow, and the shops were crowded, making rescue difficult. The fire spread for three hours, destroying as many as eighteen neighboring buildings. A portion of the Xiaoshijie Amusement Park was also affected. Details are described below:

Gas Stove Fire

The Wang Baofeng Yang Emerald Jewelry and Toy Store at No. 16 Liangting Road, Nanshi, is opened by Wang Yuquan (35 years old) from Zhenjiang. The business has been booming. At around 7:45 yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out in the upstairs of the store, due to cooking breakfast. Because all the goods and raw materials in the store were flammable, the fire quickly spread.

Fire Departments Arrive

The nearby police reported to the fire department, and the fire was already out of control. The Chenghuangmiao fire department arrived first. Seeing that the fire was getting fiercer and spreading, almost all the fire departments in Nanshi dispatched to assist in the rescue. The fire was slightly weaker at 10 o'clock. The Chenghuangmiao and Laobeidou police stations dispatched a large number of police officers to maintain order.

Child Thrown, Burned to Death

When the fire first broke out, Wang Yuquan and his wife Wang woke up from their sleep. The ladder had been burned off. In a hurry, Wang first threw his five-year-old son Da Shuangzi from the upstairs window. He and his wife and partner Zhu Yongsheng (23 years old from Zhenjiang) jumped out of the window. All three were seriously injured and sent to Nanyang Hospital. The most tragic thing was that when Wang threw Da Shuangzi down, he landed behind the horizontal sign on the door and was burned to death. Yao is seven months pregnant and her life is in danger. In addition, Wang's relative Yao Meixiao was also slightly injured and discharged from the hospital after being bandaged.

Neighbors Affected

In this fire, a total of twelve stores were burned on Liangting Road, two on Sanlin Road, two on Jiushi Road, one on Yuyuan Xin Road, and a part of Xiaoshijie Amusement Park on Fuyou Road. On Liangting Road, Zhou Xingtai Copperware Store at No. 14, Zhu Shaoxian Fortune Telling Shop at No. 18, Ran Furui Bird Store at No. 22, Jiang Xunfu Fortune Telling Shop at No. 23, Liu Zhenshan Bird Store at No. 24, Tongfukang Foreign Grocery at No. 27, He Fengming Bird Store at No. 31, Li Jinfeng Bird Cage Store at No. 33, Song Fuxiang Bird Cage Store at No. 35, the upper floors of Qianliang Guild Hall at No. 37, and the upper floors of Xinyi Zhai Bird Store at No. 39. On Sanlin Road, Xu Hongxing Cow Horn Domino Store at No. 4 and Mao Yongxing Domino Shop at No. 6. On Jiushi Road, Shunji Toy Store at No. 13 and Juxingchang Bird Cage Store at No. 15. On Yuyuan Xin Road, two upstairs rooms of Yongchun Flower Shop at No. 31. At the Xiaoshijie Amusement Park at No. 234 Fuyou Road, the rear part of the Beijing Opera Theater, four three-story buildings, the western half, and the front four- and five-story buildings were destroyed. Afterwards, the police station telegraphed to the General Bureau, cleared the remaining fire, and investigated the cause of the fire and aftermath.

He knew that carrying a fake passport was a serious crime, so he wanted to burn it, but stopped temporarily because he wanted to find out who had framed him by putting the passport in his luggage. His testimony was the same as what he said before he was imprisoned, but the judge did not believe what the defendant said and repeatedly asked him to tell the truth.

International Art Theatre Society to Perform the Opera "Dodder Dreams"

According to a report from the National News Agency's Shanghai office on the 9th, the International Art Theatre Society of Shanghai, organized by Chinese and foreign stage artists, with support from Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke and his wife, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng and his wife, Academia Sinica President Cai Yuanpei, and Central Supervisory Committee member Chu Minyi and his wife, will stage the opera "Dodder Dreams," the latest masterpiece by renowned composer Afu Xiaoloomov, at the Grand Shanghai Theatre on the 15th of this month at 7:15 p.m. Tickets are priced at four, three, and one yuan, and all proceeds will be donated to a relief fund for unemployed musicians and playwrights in Shanghai. The entire opera is divided into three acts, with elegant music, bizarre plot, and specially made costumes and sets. The entire performance is meticulously guided by experts in Chinese opera, and all movements are sufficient to express the meaning of the music and match the rhythm of the music. Rehearsals are now complete. It is expected that the performance of this opera will shine uniquely in the drama world. Composer Afu has lived in China for more than ten years, and has been dedicated to studying Chinese music and drama, keenly observing its strengths and weaknesses. He then proceeded to thoroughly explore ways to improve and develop it. Afu often said that China has extremely rich melodies, such as folk songs, etc., but unfortunately, they are only the rudiments of musical pieces, and the inner details are complex, with flaws and merits interspersed. If composers can remove the dross and select the essence, and use Western composition methods to compose large pieces, then Chinese music can stand out in the world music scene and compete with advanced European music countries. However, Western harmony, counterpoint, and musical forms are not all applicable to Chinese music. Musicians must conduct long-term research and experimentation on both Chinese and Western music to understand the way to choose what to follow and what to discard. Empty talk on paper is unrealistic, and trying to fit square pegs into round holes is also counterproductive. Afu believes that the reform of Chinese drama should start with music because music is the foundation of opera. The difficulty in developing Chinese drama is due to the lack of music suitable for the plot and movements. Therefore, reformers of drama who only focus on improving the scenery and scripts and ignore music, their reform, which abandons the root and pursues the branches, may instead lead the development of drama itself astray, and the result will be a hybrid (neither opera nor spoken drama) drama. Now, most playwrights in China do not understand Western music, and musicians are ignorant of drama. Therefore, to reform drama, both parties must cooperate and first solve the fundamental problem. The remaining minor issues will not be difficult to resolve. Afu's ideal is like this. He has composed more than ten kinds of symphonies, sonatas, preludes, and operas based on his years of research, which have been performed in Shanghai and Europe and the United States, and have attracted the attention of the music and drama circles and have received good reviews from art authorities. This performance of the opera "Dodder Dreams" will not only be welcomed by those who love music and art, but also be regarded as a valuable research material by those engaged in the movement to reform Chinese opera.

Playwright: Afu Xiaoloomov; Performers: Mr. and Mrs. Tang Shixuan

Since the bandits invaded Suiyuan, all Chinese employees of the National Customs, considering that the National Army was guarding the territory and fighting bloody battles, and their hard work and great achievements, took the lead in voluntarily donating one million yuan of their salaries and directly telegraphed it to Suiyuan, requesting Chairman Fu to forward it to the front lines to comfort them. The original letter stated, "To all Chinese employees of the National Customs, We have received your remittance of 10,000 yuan, which fully expresses your patriotic enthusiasm to encourage morale. We accept it with reverence. It is our duty to promote benevolence and vigorously encourage our troops, hoping that the three armies will be energized and devote themselves to the battlefield. Based on this sincerity, we will answer the generous gift of our patriotic compatriots. In addition to informing all units at the front, we have specially drawn up a receipt, which is sent with the letter for your perusal. As for the detailed distribution method in the future, we will declare the purpose after it is finalized, so as to show great faith. This is to express our gratitude. Sincerely wish you well. Attached is a receipt. Fu Zuoyi respectfully." The original telegram said, "To the Shanghai Customs Club, Your telegram has been received and read. We are grateful for your previous concern and donation to comfort the troops. In addition to our gratitude, we should immediately send a telegram to thank you. We believe that it has been perused. French Concession Detective Jin Jiulin Retires

Jin Jiulin, the inspector of the special agency of the French Concession Police Department, has been in office for 27 years, repeatedly solving major cases with outstanding achievements, and has always had good relationships with all parties. Now, due to old age and physical weakness, the burden is heavy and difficult to bear, so he submitted his resignation to the French Police Superintendent. Wuben Principal Sued by Teachers for Breach of Contract, Demanding Compensation for Salaries Due

Hu Lan (female), the principal of the Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School, was recently sued in court by female teachers Peng Junshi (from Jiangsu), Wan Rong (from Hubei), De Jingwa (from Liaoning), and Yan Qingxin (from Hebei), who hired lawyer Zhang Shanle, on charges of breaching the contract. Judge Pang opened the court yesterday to hear the case. The plaintiffs stated that they were hired by the defendant as teachers of the school, and submitted a request to the Municipal Education Bureau for approval and signed a contract. In the autumn of this year, the defendant suddenly stopped our work. When we asked for the reason, the defendant remained silent. In addition to reporting the defendant's abuse of private power and breach of contract to the Municipal Education Bureau, we have filed a complaint requesting compensation for the salaries due according to the law. The defendant, Hu Lan, did not appear, but was represented by the school secretary, Mr. Hu. He replied that the contract mentioned by the plaintiffs was approved by the Municipal Education Bureau, and they requested compensation, etc. However, the current teachers of the school were also approved by the Municipal Education Bureau. There was no abuse of power or suspension of their work, so they were unwilling to compensate. The judge, noting that both parties held different views, considered that mediation was unsuccessful and ordered the plaintiffs to formally file a lawsuit, and then adjourned the court.

Natural Hotel Busts Gambling Case

Yesterday, Huatan Sun Dafa and Cao Qishan of the Zhabei Police Station learned that a gambling operation specializing in copper coins, etc., was being organized in Room 308 of the Natural Hotel on Zhizhong Road. They secretly went there in the afternoon and arrested 25 gambling criminals, including Sun Weiting, Weng Ashun, Wang Ada, and Yin Renlei. Another gambling criminal, Wu Xiaolong, jumped out of the window to escape, resulting in a head injury and was sent to the hospital for treatment. The 25 gambling criminals, together with the gambling tools and foreign coins, were taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu filed a lawsuit according to the law. After Judge Pan interrogated each of the defendants, he ordered Wang Xiaolong and Sun Weiting to be detained for further investigation and ordered Wang Ada and Yin Renlei to be sentenced to three months in prison and fined 50 yuan each. The remaining 22 people, including Weng Ashun, were fined 50 yuan and 30 yuan each. The gambling tools were confiscated.

New Year's Cards and Invitation Cards Must Be Mailed Separately

According to Shanghai postal authorities, as the end of the year approaches, the number of New Year's cards and other postal items received by the post office will inevitably become crowded. If senders can bundle the three types of items separately (those sent to the local area, domestic, and overseas) and then mail them, the delivery will definitely be faster. Also, if invitation cards are to be mailed, it is best to bundle them separately and not mix them with New Year's cards to avoid delays.

Record of the Autumn Ancestral Ceremony of the Lu Clan Shrine

The Lu Clan Shrine in Laiyidu, Pudong, also known as the Lu Wenyu Public Shrine, held an autumn ancestral ceremony the day before yesterday and also convened a clan assembly, with a lively gathering, an unprecedented event in decades. At 10:00 a.m., the ancestral ceremony was held, with proper rituals. Then, a clan assembly was convened, and Lu Zhiqing was publicly elected as the chairman. First, the chairman reported on the significance of resuming the autumn ancestral ceremony, the purpose of convening the meeting, and the progress of the public property management committee's work. After the report, clan members Lu Wenshao and Lu Yuxiang successively expressed their opinions. Then, the proposal was discussed, and the entire meeting unanimously passed six resolutions. The meeting adjourned when the clock struck one. Immediately afterward, a banquet was held, and after the meal, photos were taken, and clan members went to the tombs of their ancestors to pay respects until about 4:00 p.m., when the clan members bid farewell.

Central Bank Inspection Report

The three hundred and twelfth inspection report on the issuance reserve of Central Bank convertible notes states: This council, in accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, is responsible for inspecting the amount of convertible notes issued by the bank and its reserves. The 312th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the bank on December 5th of the 25th year of the Republic of China. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 31,434,6458 silver dollars, including 17,602,9952 silver dollar notes and 3,831,6506 subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of convertible note reserves is 31,434,6458 silver dollars, including 20,550,06958 silver dollars in cash reserves. Among the cash reserves, 92,894,358.48 silver dollars are deposited in the bank's issuing branches and sub-branches, and 11,261,2599.52 silver dollars are deposited with other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 10,883,9500 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 400,09630.07 customs gold units. The total amount of customs gold convertible note reserves is 400,09630.07 customs gold units. This reserve includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68, equivalent to 400,09630.07 customs gold units. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve shall be at least 60%, and the remainder shall be guaranteed by legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. December 7th, 25th year of the Republic of China. Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank: Li Fuxun, Supervisors: Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiluo.

Common Sense on Self-Treatment

The Threat of Winter to Bone Pain Sufferers

— Doctor Yu Bofu

The severe winter is indeed a cause for concern for the sick. From a medical standpoint, the impact on bone pain sufferers is particularly severe. Every year, sufferers not only experience increased pain during this cold winter, but also, due to weakened resistance, may even suffer from contractures of the limbs and abnormal numbness. Furthermore, those who are usually affected by rheumatism are able to withstand it because their resistance is able to hold up against it, thus avoiding the suffering of joint pain. However, once winter arrives, due to the harsh climate, everything falls into a state of decline, and resistance is also weakened. Therefore, the encroachment of rheumatism becomes unrestrained, causing damage everywhere, resulting in back pain, joint numbness, and various other symptoms erupting one after another. Therefore, this time is the most threatening for bone pain sufferers. However, with proper defense, not only can bone pain be avoided, but even those who have already contracted it can be completely cured. I have repeatedly tested this, and it is accurate to the slightest detail. This method should be used when one feels a lack of energy. At the beginning of winter, quickly take the reproductive gland hormone preparation "Reproductin" to replenish physical strength, so that the body's resistance is not disrupted by seasonal changes. At the same time, take "Strongston's Bone Pain Tablets," which have the functions of dispelling wind, removing dampness, purifying blood, and preventing arteriosclerosis, then the patient will definitely feel relaxed joints and completely eliminate pain.

Exciting Beyond Expectations, Jinan Lost by Only Three Points, Defeated by Xintong 26 to 29, The Outcome of the Last Four Minutes Still Uncertain

In the Xiqing Basketball Independent Group match, Jinan faced Xintong. The fierce battle ended last night, with Jinan unfortunately defeated by Xintong by a margin of three points, 26 to 29. In the first half, Jinan led by two points with a score of 14 to 12. Although Jinan lost, the performance was truly unexpectedly exciting. Xintong fought fiercely, only surpassing Jinan in the last four minutes. In those last four minutes, the score fluctuated closely, with each team scoring one point alternately for a long time. Thanks to Bersell's one successful free throw, Xintong was able to win by three points with a score of 29 to 26. The hardships endured during the game were evident, and the victory was not easily achieved. As for Jinan, they had a great opportunity to win last night, leading by as many as eight points at one point. However, due to a careless mistake, they allowed Xintong to take advantage of the opportunity to rise. Wang Nanzhen's performance was outstanding, and the center, Kuang Yao'ya, was fouled out, which was a fatal blow at the final moment. The Xiqing venue was packed, and in the last few minutes, the dramatic changes made everyone restless and extremely tense. It is hoped that Jinan will be able to retaliate in the second round. Unfortunately, Between One Careless Moment, Bersell Shi Guiya Karl Went on a Consecutive Scoring Spree with Free Throws, Scoring Six Points in One Go, and Xintong Managed to Catch Up to 14 to 12 in the First Half, Jinan Leading by Only One Point.

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Commends Guangdong East Middle School for Its Achievements, Which Are Classified As Grade A

Guangdong East Middle School (Formerly Guangzhao Middle School) on Zhabei Hydropower Road Is Managed Conscientiously and Has Outstanding Achievements. In The Education Bureau's Inspection Report for the 23rd Year, The School's Achievements Were Classified As Grade A And Have Been Commended. The School Has Now Received Instructions From the Social Affairs Bureau, Hai Zi No. 5405, Which State: "The Case Is Checked and Accepted According to the Previous Education Bureau's Inspection Report on Private Secondary Schools in the 24th Year, The School's Land Covers a Vast Area of More Than 200 Mu, The School Building Design Is Detailed, The School Affairs Planning Is Very Organized, And The Training And Education Implementation Is Also Achieved With Achievements, Which Can Be Used As an Example by Other Schools," Cheng Ji Is Listed As Grade A And Should Be Commended To Encourage It. This Order』, The School Recently Published An Overview and School Publication of Shanghai Guangdong East Middle School, The Materials Are Very Rich And Can Be Used As a Reference for The Education Community.

Cultural Circle - Support Suiyuan Movement

Municipal People's Education Center: The Municipal People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road in this city has monthly activity centers. This month, in order to support the anti-bandit soldiers in Suiyuan in the freezing cold, in addition to arranging a vigilant environment for supporting Suiyuan's anti-banditry in the center, it specifically organized the Suiyuan Anti-Bandit Support Association and the Fundraising Committee the day before yesterday. It is reported that the center held its second committee meeting yesterday, chaired by Zai Chunxi. Discussion items, in addition to stepping up publicity efforts, also established a fundraising committee, and elected standing committee members, including Xu Zexiang, Zai Chunxi, Zheng Yufeng, Liu Ruichang, Long Yingjie, Chen Nianhui, and Yu Jian, to take charge of the matter. Fundraising methods include setting up a donation counter at the entrance of the center, with a large map of the Suiyuan war zone and an explanatory sign hanging next to it. Donors can choose whether to register their names or not. Those who do not want to register their names can directly throw the money into the counter. Those who wish to register their names are requested to hand over the donation directly to the savings office jointly run by the center and the China Reclamation Bank, which will issue receipts. As for publicity methods, there are two types: lectures and quick reports. The lecture time is from 9:00 am to 10:00 am and from 1:00 pm to 2:00 pm every day. The center will send staff to give lectures in rotation. The quick report is to summarize the front-line war situation at 6:30 am every day and announce it at the entrance of the center to awaken the public and understand the bandit situation and the invasion of the rebels. The lecture topics of the center include: the latest progress of the Suiyuan anti-banditry situation and the understanding that citizens should have; "The Suiyuan situation after the National Army recovered Lingmiao"; "The international situation and Sino-Japanese disputes"; "The Japanese naval situation in the Pacific"; "The responsibilities that the public should bear in extraordinary times"; "Predicting the results of pseudo-bandits from the three aspects of favorable timing, geographical advantages, and popular support." As for fundraising, as of the 8th of this month, a total of 21 yuan, 3 jiao, and 8 fen have been received, including 4 yuan, 1 jiao, and 5 fen of silver dollars, 20 jiao of small silver dollars, 1 jiao and 17 fen of legal tender, and 43,080 copper coins.

The Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association's Ninth Elementary School launched the Suiyuan Support Association the week before last, and has been actively carrying out the work in recent days, raising a total of 100 yuan and 1 fen of national currency. In addition to handing over the full amount to the Shen Bao for remittance, it will continue to carry out the work to fulfill its national duties.

Baptist Mingde Elementary School: Students of all grades of the Baptist Mingde Elementary School in Laobeimen, this port, in view of the soldiers at the front line of Suiyuan killing bandits and defending the country, and motivated by patriotic indignation, save fruit every day, and the proceeds are transferred to support Suiyuan's donation. Yesterday, they sent 25 yuan, 7 jiao, and 3 fen of donation to this newspaper for remittance to the front.

Minguang Middle School: Yu Xianglin and other students of Minguang Middle School on Jiaozhou Road in this city convened an emergency meeting of grade leaders a few days ago to discuss the organization of a comfort association for anti-bandit soldiers in Suiyuan. They have already sent 80 yuan and 8 fen of donations from teachers and students to the front.

National Zhejiang University of Hangzhou: The Department of History and Geography of the university, in order to make the citizens of Hangzhou understand the geographical situation of the province due to the Suiyuan incident and to encourage anti-banditry, held the Suiyuan Provincial Map Exhibition at the university from the 1st to the 3rd of this month. The exhibits were divided into three categories: maps, books, and photographs, totaling about 200 items, which were dazzling and beautiful. On the eve of the opening, Zhang Qiyun, the head of the department, gave a lecture on "The Military Geography of Suiyuan Province." No less than 1,200 people listened. Moreover, according to statistics, more than 1,000 people visited in total in three days. After the closing, it was borrowed by the Zhejiang Provincial Library for display for three days, and there were also many viewers.

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to Investigate School-Age Children Starting Tomorrow - Preparation for Promoting Compulsory Education - Investigation Period Set for Three Weeks, Ending at the End of the Month

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau regards the promotion of compulsory education as an important plan for the revival of China, and the investigation of school-age children is the basis for the promotion of compulsory education. This city has a dense population and a large number of school children. In order to understand the situation of school-age children and to promote compulsory education, the bureau has decided to investigate school-age children in the city from the 11th to the 31st of this month. The bureau has assigned teachers and staff of municipal elementary schools and a part of private schools, as well as senior students, to be responsible for the investigation. The investigators wear investigation certificates for identification. The bureau has already issued a bulletin to inform the residents of the city, and residents are requested to report truthfully when they meet the investigators.
